Institute of Pacific Relations: Hu Shih Points out that Japan is Obstructing Our Construction; China is Seeking Self-Reliance; Japanese Representative to Respond Today

Yosemite: The sixth conference of the Institute of Pacific Relations continued yesterday afternoon. First, the Chinese representative, Dr. Hu Shih, Dean of the Faculty of Arts of Peking University in China, delivered a speech, severely criticizing Japan's policy towards China. He stated, "Any Chinese government that is powerful enough to unify the country and enhance its national status will not be tolerated by Japan. This has almost become a fixed policy in Japan." Therefore, Japan is responsible for China's difficult situation. The Chinese nation is now determined to fight to the end to maintain its own survival. As far as the three northeastern provinces are concerned, Japan's military occupation of the area has created a state of war with China. Not only is China's economic reconstruction movement being obstructed, but also the cooperation between other countries and China is unable to proceed. The intention is to prevent the revival of the Chinese nation. After Hu Shih's speech, the Japanese representative immediately stood up to express his opposition and stated that he would respond point by point tomorrow. (Havas dispatch, 25th)

Yosemite: The Institute of Pacific Relations continued its conference today. Chinese representative Dr. Hu Shih stated in his speech that China has recognized that all kinds of world peace organizations have been destroyed beyond repair. China must rely on its own efforts in the future. As for the three principles of Japanese Prime Minister Hirota, Hu Shih declared that Japan's ultimate goal is clearly to completely control China politically, but China is determined to continue fighting. An independent China is now engaged in the construction of railways, aviation, education, and disaster relief as a material foundation for national unification. China currently has 100,000 kilometers of railways, which the National Government was able to use to suppress the Communist Party and the previous rebellion in Fujian. As for the nature of Sino-Russian relations, only time will tell. Pierson, a member of the US Foreign Policy Association, declared that the best way to solve the China problem is for all countries to agree to allow China to build with peace of mind, without the need to resist foreign aggression by force. Expert Tyler stated that China's economy, society, and culture are undergoing drastic changes, and it is difficult to predict the future, but international relations will inevitably become more complicated as a result. The progress of China's construction is extremely unbalanced, and it does not have a predetermined goal and a consistent plan like Soviet Russia. Its steps change with the situation. Although there has been considerable progress in politics, economic construction has not developed in a balanced way. The dualism of government agencies is sufficient to hinder progress. But politically, China is a whole country. The organs and symbols of the central government's power, such as the national defense forces, national banks, tax collection agencies, and airports in major cities, are all sufficient to indicate change and progress. This new organization will obviously make the international situation more complicated, and its stability will be affected by the politics and situation of various countries. The Chinese representative also read out a paper on China's new monetary policy and the recent development of China's cotton industry to the conference, and asked the representatives to pay attention to the fierce competition between Japanese spinning mills and Chinese merchants. (National Telegraph, 24th)

Yosemite: The Chinese representative declared to the Pacific Conference today that China welcomes assistance from all countries for its construction, but does not want Japanese interference. The Japanese representative immediately refuted this, insisting that China's only hope is in unity and construction, and Japan's only wish is to cooperate with China. The Chinese representative also replied that Japan often transmits the idea of cooperation to the Chinese people but the Chinese people are unable to understand the true meaning of their cooperation. The US representative declared that while the United States has always respected China's sovereignty, it should also consider the most-favored-nation clause. This clause has forced China to sign the majority of international treaties, damaging its sovereignty. The Chinese representative also stated that the Canadian Overseas Chinese Bank has lent US$500,000 to support China's construction, but Japan does not want China to negotiate loans with foreign countries. China will never again make political concessions or allow outsiders to discuss the statement made by the Japanese Foreign Ministry spokesman that foreign countries are not allowed to interfere in Chinese affairs. (National Telegraph, 24th)

Yosemite: The Japanese representative to the Pacific Institute today afternoon requested a special meeting to be convened on Tuesday in order to respond to the Chinese representative's remarks that Japan is obstructing China's recovery. (National Telegraph, 24th)

Ambassador Guo Talks About Our Country Clearing Foreign Debts; Payment of Interest on the Longhai and Guangzhou-Kowloon Bonds; Major Articles Published in London Newspapers

(London) Today, this newspaper's reporter visited Mr. Guo Taiqi, the Chinese Ambassador to the UK, and discussed the recent clearing of loans and the fact that Chinese bonds are now more popular than they were a few years ago. Ambassador Guo responded, "China has indeed made progress and is worthy of great respect." The editors of London's financial publications have all published the news of the recent clearing of foreign debts in prominent positions. "The Financial Times" published an article by Dr. Pan, Secretary-General of the Chinese Ministry of Railways, solemnly stating the Chinese government's emphasis on clearing various debts and restoring national credit, and especially hoping to obtain new funds for the construction of new railways. He also stated that the Chinese government has great sincerity towards all creditors and hopes that creditors can show the same spirit in negotiations and recognize the changes in China and the world situation. In recent months, various circles here have had an optimistic view of the current situation in China. Nanjing's swift handling of the Southwest Incident has given a good impression here. Many observers say that since the February 26 Tokyo Incident this year, Japan's policy towards China has not been as disruptive as before. A few observers expressed regret over the cancellation of some railway debts, but still welcomed the various agreements reached between the Chinese government and bondholders, because they have a clear understanding of China's difficulties and its desire to repay the debts as soon as possible. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

(London) The London Stock Exchange's reaction to the Chinese government's declaration of resuming interest payments on the Longhai and Guangzhou-Kowloon railway bonds has been inconsistent. Because rumors that the Longhai railway loan would soon resume interest payments have been circulating for a long time, the immediate impact of this declaration was only a slight drop in the price of the bonds. Several parties expressed disappointment that the interest rate did not exceed 1.5% at the beginning. As for the market, it believes that the current trend of Longhai railway bonds is due to too many buyers, resulting in the exhausted bulls being liquidated. On the other hand, some believe that the interest on the Longhai bonds will be at least equal to the interest paid on the Guangzhou-Kowloon bonds within two years. This is why Longhai bonds sell better than Guangzhou-Kowloon bonds. The sudden rise in the price of Guangzhou-Kowloon bonds from around £33 to £42 in recent days has surprised many people, because it was generally expected that the bonds would not pay 2% or 1.5% interest in the short term. However, the market believes that the different price trends of the above two bonds are due to the difference in the total amount in circulation in the market. Currently, the amount of Guangzhou-Kowloon bonds that have not been paid is only £171,000 in interest and £940,000 in principal, while Longhai bonds have as much as £4,000,000. The current selling price of Longhai bonds is £32, while the buying price of Guangzhou-Kowloon bonds is £42. (Reuters dispatch, 25th)

Japanese Cabinet Decides on Important National Policies, Divided into Seven Categories

(Tokyo) Based on the statement made when the cabinet was formed, in order to reform the administration and establish important national policies, the government has organized and adopted the following policies from the more than 30 national policies proposed by various ministries, and the cabinet announced their content on the 25th.

(1) Strengthening national defense.

(2) Refreshing and improving education.

(3) Reorganizing the central and local tax systems.

(4) Stabilizing the people's livelihood: (1) Disaster prevention policies, (2) Establishing insurance facilities, (3) Promoting the economy of rural villages and the economy of small and medium-sized high-tech industries.

(5) Promoting industry and expanding trade: (1) Controlling and strengthening electricity, (2) Needs and supplies of liquid fuels and iron and steel, (3) Ensuring fiber resources, (4) Controlling trade, (5) Promoting aviation and shipping industries, (6) Assisting the development of Japanese expatriates overseas.

(6) Establishing important policies towards Manchuria.

(7) Organizing and improving the administrative structure. (Domei dispatch, 25th)

(Tokyo) The regular cabinet meeting held on the 25th to decide on the new national policies of the Hirota Cabinet began at 9:30 AM at the Prime Minister's official residence. After deciding on the items of important national policies, Prime Minister Hirota rose to express his views, saying that among the policies proposed by various ministers, those that are considered important and related to the budget should be approved as listed in the attached document. He also hoped that the bills related to this matter would be prepared urgently. Regarding matters related to various ministries, he hoped that the ministries would carefully discuss and draft specific plans, and those that are not related to the budget should also be studied and implemented, such as the Ministry of Justice's research, investigation, and organization of laws and regulations. Then, two or three cabinet members spoke, saying that the national policy items need to be more specific. As a result, the decision on the items was the first step towards making them concrete in the future. The scope of the national policies decided by the current cabinet is limited, so following the Prime Minister's explanation, after the decision, Minister of Justice Hayashi asked, what measures will be taken for those not included in the national policy items? The Prime Minister and Minister of Finance replied that they would consider them appropriately. The meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM. (Domei dispatch, 25th)

(Paris) Regarding the agreement on non-interference in the Spanish civil unrest proposed by France, Germany has already responded, promising to prohibit the shipment of arms to Spain. Official sources here have expressed satisfaction with this reply. However, just as one wave subsides, another rises. Germany has suddenly decided to extend the length of military service, and the general public believes that this move will add another factor of unrest to the European situation. Therefore, the sense of satisfaction has been diminished at once. France, England, Germany, Belgium, and Czechoslovakia are all arms-manufacturing countries. Now, they are all competing to agree to the conclusion of an agreement of non-interference in the Spanish civil unrest. Italy, due to two reservations, is still hesitant, but in view of Germany's decision, it should follow suit without further consideration. Some people here advocate that countries that have already implemented arms embargoes should send representatives to hold a meeting to discuss everything, so that the authorities of various countries, once the Spanish issue has a concrete solution, can step up preparations for the next League of Nations General Assembly and the Locarno Five-Power Conference. However, this kind of situation has become commonplace in Irun, and people no longer pay attention to it. Revised Prices for Domestic Telegrams

(Nanjing) It was reported a few days ago that the Ministry of Communications had revised the prices for domestic telegrams. The reporter recently inquired with the Ministry of Communications and obtained accurate information: (1) Domestic telegrams were originally divided into within-province and out-of-province. Since the 17th year, they were revised to be the same nationwide, one dime per word. Now, the ministry believes that this method is slightly unfair, and it has been decided that from September 1st, it will be changed back to seven cents per word within the province, and out-of-province telegrams will still be charged one dime per word. (2) The method of calculating the fees for the address of Chinese telegrams has also been revised. Previously, it was originally stipulated that the name and address of the recipient within 15 characters would be charged as five characters. Now, it has been changed to one character for every two characters, and the remaining number of characters less than two characters is also counted as one character. It applies equally to both within-province and out-of-province telegrams. (Central News Agency Telegram, 25th)

Joint Memorial Week of the Guangdong Party, Government, and Military: Full Text of Chairman Chiang's Report

Guangzhou News - The full text of Chairman Chiang's report at the Guangdong Joint Memorial Week on the 24th is as follows:

Fellow Comrades, today, taking advantage of the opportunity of this memorial week, I will give you a brief report on my views on "Building Guangdong into a Model Province of the Three Principles of the People." Now, how are we going to work hard to improve the current situation in Guangdong and build a model province of the Three Principles of the People? Of course, all comrades from the Party, Government, Military, and Education must work hard to ensure that Party affairs are sound, politics are clear, military affairs are organized, and education and the economy are developed. In particular, we must earnestly achieve the three primary tasks that Zhongzheng said: (1) eradicate poverty and filth, (2) prohibit opium and gambling, and (3) never seize the people's interests. However, I believe that everyone has paid close attention to these matters and is working hard to do them, so I will not repeat them. What Zhongzheng wants to say today is what is the active and fundamental task that comrades from the Party, Government, Military, and Education should jointly strive for in the future to build a model province of the Three Principles of the People? In other words, where should we start building at the beginning? I think that the most important and urgent task among the myriad of tasks is to build a new province, social order, and create a new social atmosphere, that is, to change the atmosphere and revitalize people's hearts. Since Zhongzheng arrived in Guangdong, I have felt that in the past two weeks, due to the joint efforts of comrades from the Party, Government, and Military, the entire social order of Guangdong has been restored, and everything is relatively organized. However, everyone must know that what we have done now is only restoring the original old order, and we have not further built a new order of modern society. The old order that has been restored now is almost the same as the situation in the former Qing era twenty or thirty years ago. This is not the order of modern society that I am talking about. Therefore, in the future, we must go further and build the new order of modern society in Guangdong very quickly. Specifically, it is to ask everyone to reform all the bad customs, habits, thoughts, and actions of the past, change the old order to the new order, change the old atmosphere to the new atmosphere, and change the old life to the new life. We must do this first, and then all aspects of construction work can be quickly promoted, and the model province of the Three Principles of the People can be built as soon as possible. Everyone must know that to build a modern country, we do not necessarily need sophisticated weapons and powerful military equipment. The most important thing is that the general public has noble morals and the entire country has a noble personality. As long as the personality of our general public and the entire country can be improved, even without sophisticated weapons and powerful military equipment, foreigners will not dare to despise us, let alone invade us. We will definitely be able to build an independent and free modern country of the Three Principles of the People. For example, there are many small countries in Europe that do not have strong military power, and even do not have troops in the country, only police. However, because the morals of their general public are very rich, and the personality of the entire country is also improved as a result, they are respected. The neighboring imperialists cannot despise him even if they want to, and they do not dare to invade him. This is the most obvious example. The ancients said, "People must insult themselves before others insult them." The reason why we are so humiliated and invaded by others now, fundamentally speaking, is not because we have too few troops and poor weapons. It is really because our general public is backward in knowledge, especially because our morals have fallen, and there are too many weaknesses in all aspects of life habits, thoughts, and actions. Because of self-humiliation, we invite foreign insults. Therefore, to resist foreign insults and build a modern country, we must rectify the source, improve the moral personality of the general public, that is, to build a modern social order, and fundamentally improve the status of our country. This is the path we must follow to build a country, and it is also the key point of our efforts to build a model province of the Three Principles of the People in the future. Everyone may feel that the truth I am talking about is too superficial and empty, and it does not seem that simple and easy to enrich national power and avoid invasion. However, I want to tell you that if we want to build a modern country, we cannot start without first improving the moral personality of the general public. Especially to build a model province of the Three Principles of the People in Guangdong, according to my research results in the past two weeks, I believe that the first important thing at present is to hurry up and build a new Guangzhou, that is, to transform the social order of Guangzhou, in order to change the atmosphere of Guangzhou and revitalize the hearts of the people of the whole country. Apart from this, there is no other way. (To be continued)

Educational Broadcasting Special Issue

Effective Methods for Preventing Rice Stem Borers, Aphids, and Locusts (Part 2)

— Wu Fuzhen, Dean of the College of Agriculture, Zhejiang University

1. Timely Implementation is Key For example, lighting lamps must be done when rice stem borer moths first appear. Otherwise, most moths have already laid eggs, making it useless to lure and kill them. Similarly, egg collection must be done at the first sign of egg laying. Otherwise, most of the eggs have already hatched, and collecting empty egg masses is of little practical benefit.

2. Cooperation is Essential If lamps are lit in one area but not in others, moths from all areas will gather in the illuminated area, causing rice paddies near the lights to be covered in egg masses. Similarly, if eggs are collected in one area but not in others, rice stem borers in the uncollected areas will mature into moths and fly to the collected area, diminishing the effectiveness of egg collection.

3. Thorough Implementation is Necessary Rice stem borers have an extremely high reproductive rate, as mentioned earlier. If egg collection, moth capture, and rice root digging are not done thoroughly, the remaining few stem borers will quickly multiply to a very large number. Farmers often say that rice stem borer control is futile because the work is not thorough enough.

(B) Aphids

Aphids have different names in different regions, such as "greasy bugs" or "oily bugs." There are many types, some harming various vegetables, some harming various fruit trees, and some harming various crops. However, their life habits are mostly similar, so the control methods are also similar. The common cotton aphid will now be used as an example:

(1) The Life Cycle of an Aphid

Aphids are insects with gradual metamorphosis, having three stages in their life: egg, nymph, and adult. Adults have winged and wingless forms due to seasonal changes and migration. They reproduce through live birth and egg laying, and their reproductive rate is very high, with two to three dozen generations per year. They usually reproduce through live birth in the spring, and the aphids born are all females. These mother aphids can give birth without mating with males. This method of reproduction is called parthenogenesis. A mother aphid can produce an average of 33 offspring. When the climate is suitable and food is abundant, the offspring can reproduce a second generation of aphids after four or five days. If we do an ideal calculation of this reproduction rate, assuming that a mother aphid's offspring, from May to September, all grow up, the number of descendants would reach 2,345,734,188,000,000,000,000,000,000,000. If these cotton aphids are calculated at one cubic millimeter per individual, the accumulated volume would be larger than the Earth. This great reproductive power is truly frightening! Therefore, if there are one or two cotton aphids in a cotton field, they must be quickly eliminated, otherwise the field will soon be full of them.

Live-born females are mostly wingless, but when it is time to migrate, winged females will be produced to move from one place to another. In late October, parthenogenesis stops, and male and female aphids are produced. Males are winged, and females are wingless. After mating, they lay eggs. A female aphid lays 11-12 eggs at most and 3-4 eggs at least. These eggs overwinter on plants in the field. In March of the following year, when the weather warms up, they hatch into the first generation of female aphids, which parasitize shepherd's purse and reproduce offspring through parthenogenesis. Later, they migrate to cotton or various melons to cause harm.

(2) Effective Control Methods for Aphids

Based on the above description, aphid control methods can be divided into two steps: first, egg removal; and second, insect removal.

(1) Egg Removal The peak period for cotton aphids to lay eggs is in mid-November. If we pull out the cotton stalks before they lay eggs, dry them, and burn them as fuel, we can reduce the opportunity for egg laying. After the cotton stalks are removed, winter plowing should be carried out to bury the remaining cotton branches and leaves in the soil. At the same time, weeds along the edge of the field should be removed and burned to eliminate overwintering aphid eggs and prevent aphid outbreaks the following year.

Overwintering aphid eggs hatch in March. After hatching, they mostly parasitize on shepherd's purse. Therefore, if we remove and burn this weed in early spring, we can eliminate even the remaining overwintering aphid eggs.

(2) Insect Removal Insect removal means eliminating aphid nymphs and adults. Because aphids are very small and have sucking mouthparts, we must use a pesticide that can kill them on contact. There are many types of pesticides, but the following three are the most effective and economical:

A. Cotton Oil Emulsion The formula is one jin of soap, two jin of clear water, and two and a half jin of cotton oil. Preparation method: First, cut the soap into small pieces, add water, and boil until dissolved. At the same time, put the cotton oil in a pot and heat it slowly. When the cotton oil is heated to near boiling (around 70 degrees Celsius), slowly pour it into the hot soapy liquid and stir rapidly with a wooden stick until thoroughly mixed and the mixture becomes a semi-liquid emulsion. This liquid is the stock solution and must be diluted 80 times with water before application. When diluting, first add two to three times the volume of warm water slowly and stir rapidly with a wooden stick until thoroughly mixed, then add cold water to reach 80 times the original volume. This diluted emulsion must be sprayed on the insects using a sprayer, otherwise it will be ineffective. Cotton aphids usually gather on the underside of leaves, so it is best to use a curved leaf-bottom spray nozzle when spraying. Sprayers are available at the Central Agricultural Industrial Institute. They are lightweight, flexible, and reasonably priced. You can go there to purchase them.

B. Kerosene Emulsion The formula is one tael of soap, one jin of clear water, and two jin of kerosene. The preparation and application method can refer to the cotton oil emulsion treatment above. However, when using this agent, dilute it with water 30 to 40 times.

C. Tobacco Water Take one jin of tobacco leaves, add 15 jin of water, and soak overnight to make tobacco water. Spraying it on aphids with a sprayer can also kill them.

The raw materials for the above three pesticides are readily available everywhere, and preparation and application are also very convenient. If you have aphids, you can choose one of them to implement prevention and control.

Today All Day: Citizens Supplement Citizen Registration Completed in 21 locations in one day Farmers' associations and trade unions schedule the election of candidates

Central News Agency: The supplementary citizen registration for all citizens will be conducted by the National Election Office from 9:00 a.m. to 5:00 p.m. today throughout the city, at 21 locations throughout the city. The locations of the supplementary registration offices were noted in yesterday's newspaper. It is expected that a large number of people will go to register nearby today.

Meaning of Registration Oath

A reporter visited the person in charge of the National Election Office yesterday. According to him, citizen registration and oath-taking are necessary procedures to implement the Prime Minister's teachings before the completion of tutelage and the beginning of constitutionalism. The meaning is to enable citizens with legal qualifications to sincerely swear an oath to support the Republic of China, implement the Three Principles of the People, and adopt the Five-Power Constitution so that when constitutionalism begins, they can be entrusted with political power and use it well. Civilized and law-abiding countries in the world all regard oath-taking as the foundation of the rule of law. Therefore, citizens who naturalize into a country must take an oath to show their sincerity, respect their national system, abide by their constitution, and strive for their obligations, and then they can be recognized as citizens. Otherwise, even if they live in the country for their entire lives, they will still be regarded as foreigners and will not be able to enjoy the rights of citizens. Therefore, unless one doubts the Republic of China or does not believe in the Republic of China, one should participate in citizen registration and oath-taking to obtain citizenship, and then one can exercise the four political powers of election, recall, initiative, and referendum and enjoy the civil rights granted by the state. However, oath-taking must begin with rectifying one's heart and having sincere intentions, and then self-cultivation and managing the state can be achieved. If one is hypocritical and perfunctory, it will not only desecrate the sanctity of the oath but also invite self-destruction. Yuan Shikai in the early Republic and Chen Jiongming in the third year of the Republic are examples of this. I hope those who perform citizen registration and oath-taking will not be negligent.

Seven Points to Note for Registration

He then said that the purpose of the supplementary citizen registration tomorrow (that is, today) is to remedy the citizens who missed the last registration, and the method is more thorough. All citizens in the city who have not yet registered should know that civil rights cannot be abandoned and should immediately go to the nearest registration office to obtain and fill out a registration form in order to wait for the summons to take the oath. However, there are several points to note: (1) Citizen registration and oath-taking are performed only once per person, so those who have already registered at their service unit, school, or organization do not need to fill out another form. (2) All those who are 20 years old or older and have resided in the city for more than one year, and who do not have any of the circumstances listed in Article 3 of the Registration Rules (such as betraying the National Government, corruption in public service, deprivation of civil rights, mental illness, opium addiction, or being under guardianship), should be registered as citizens, regardless of gender, wealth, or status. (3) In the "membership in occupational organization" column of the registration form, if you joined an organization before May 14th of this year (that is, the date the Election Law was promulgated), you should specify "Farmers' Association," "Trade Union," "Chamber of Commerce," or "Education Association," etc. Otherwise, write "None." (4) If a woman does not have a name, she should indicate "Mother/Wife/Sister/ Younger Sister of So-and-so" on the form for identification. (5) You should note your address on the registration form so that it can be investigated if necessary. (6) The registration form must be filled out by the person on the spot and returned to the registration office. The other copy of the oath can be taken back and submitted after the summons to take the oath, in exchange for a citizen certificate. (7) If you filled out a form last time but did not return it, you should take the opportunity to return it to the nearest registration office as soon as possible. I hope all citizens will pay attention to the above seven points.

Organizations Begin to Elect

According to the procedures for handling elections, the representatives of various occupational organizations should begin to elect their candidates immediately. The office has set the 27th of this month as the date for the election of candidates for the Farmers' Association (including the Fishermen's Association), with the location at the Municipal Farmers' Association. The 29th is the date for the election of candidates for the Trade Union, with the location at the General Trade Union. Notice has been given to the executive organ officials of each lowest-level organization of the relevant associations stipulated by the Election Law to attend the election at the appointed time.

Organizational Members Swear Oath

The National Election Office has also set the 27th of this month for all Trade Union members to take the citizen oath, and the 29th for Farmers' Association (including Fishermen's Association) members to take the citizen oath, with the location at each lower-level Farmers' Association and Trade Union. (The date for members of the same trade association to take the oath is still being determined.) The Farmers' Association and Trade Union have been notified so that they can participate in the election of official representatives in the future.

Election Laws Reprinted

The Municipal National Election Office previously printed a small booklet of the National Assembly Representatives Election Law and Implementing Rules promulgated by the National Government to meet the needs of all sectors. Within just over ten days, it was completely distributed. Therefore, it has been reprinted a few days ago, and the legal provisions have been carefully proofread. The interpretations of the General Office have also been compiled and included as much as possible for reference. It was published yesterday. However, not many copies have been printed. Therefore, all units, schools, and organizations that need it must send a letter with postage attached to the office to request it, and then it will be mailed accordingly.

Arrived in Shanghai the Night Before Last, Proceeding to Nanjing Tonight

Mr. He is staying at the New Asia Hotel on Tiantong Road. When he arrived in Shanghai the night before last, few people knew in advance. Only Yang Hu, the Shanghai-Wusong Garrison Commander, received a telegram from Xu Shiying, the ambassador to Japan, and went to meet him with Secretary Wang Zhinan. That evening, they hosted a welcome dinner for Mr. He at the International Hotel. Mr. He's wife and son also returned home with him. Li Yaonan, an attaché at the Turkish embassy, was transferred to the Japanese embassy and traveled with them to Japan before disembarking. Mr. He met with Zhou Jue, director of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai office, Zhang Mengling, and many others yesterday morning. He also went out to visit friends and attended a dinner hosted by relatives at noon. He plans to visit Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, today and take the night express train to Nanjing at 11 PM to report everything to Foreign Minister Zhang.

Three-Month Leave, Intends to Extend

Mr. He met with a reporter from the New Voice Society at his residence at 2:30 PM yesterday afternoon and made a statement. He began by saying that he had been serving as minister to Turkey for a year and a half and was not familiar with the situation in China. He wanted to learn about recent developments, such as the recent disturbances in Guangdong and Guangxi and various changes in the country. Therefore, he requested leave to return home for inspection, and also to attend the National Assembly, which is about to convene (Note: Mr. He is a member of the Central Committee and a natural representative), and to take care of personal matters. The original leave was for three months, but due to delays en route, he will need to extend it. He departed Turkey on the 15th of last month, traveled via Italy, crossed the Atlantic Ocean to the United States, and met with Ambassador to the United States, Shi Zhaoji. He heard that Shi Zhaoji was also planning to return home and be replaced by Wang Zhengting, but he did not discuss this. He stayed in New York for ten days, changed ships to cross the Pacific Ocean, and stopped in Japan, where he met with Ambassador to Japan, Xu Shiying, before returning home on the same ship.

Turkey Expresses Great Sympathy for China

He continued, stating that Turkish President Kemal Pasha and the general Korean population deeply sympathize with China's current situation. Before World War I, Turkey, like China, rose up as a new nation through national effort. Turkey has a history of thousands of years and is now seeking to promote its ancient culture. Tracing its origins to the Uyghur Turks, the authorities are encouraging scholars and professors to actively research Chinese culture, eliminating Arabian and Persian influences.

Turkish Foreign Affairs and Trade Situation

Mr. He continued, stating that Turkish diplomacy is well-managed. Ten years ago, Turkey established friendly relations with the Soviet Union. Recently, Great Britain also made peace with Turkey, and therefore, the issue of the straits, which Turkey considers crucial, was resolved. As for the country's trade, the situation is unique, adopting a "reciprocity system," that is, a controlled nature. Any country trading with Turkey, any country that exports goods to Turkey must import Turkish goods of equal value, with the aim of offsetting and preventing the outflow of cash.

Sino-Turkish Trade Agreement Under Negotiation

Mr. He then answered the reporter's questions, stating that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has instructed Minister to Switzerland, Hu Shize, to conduct negotiations in Geneva regarding the drafting of a Sino-Turkish trade agreement. While he was in Turkey, he also discussed it with the Turkish authorities. However, because Turkey's foreign trade adopts a "reciprocity system," China must first have an organization internally. Therefore, although there have been negotiations, there has been no decision. During this trip back to China, he will discuss this matter in detail with the government authorities, especially the Ministry of Industry. Currently, China has no commercial presence in Turkey, and there are very few overseas Chinese. Therefore, in addition to a Sino-Turkish trade agreement, a residency treaty must also be concluded, allowing citizens of both countries to freely reside in each other's countries. However, this matter has not received formal instructions from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and must be requested and decided upon during this trip back to China before proceeding.

Denies the Closure of the Turkish Embassy

When the reporter asked about rumors of the closure of the embassy in Turkey and his (referring to Mr. He) assignment to a position in China, Mr. He replied that these rumors are absolutely untrue. Turkey has also decided to send an ambassador to China. Fude Pei was previously appointed, but the plan was delayed due to budget issues. It was not until July of this year that it was approved by the cabinet. The candidate must be reappointed. He deeply feels that diplomatic affairs must be handled by specialized personnel, and he fears that he is not competent enough. After he returns to China, the embassy affairs will be temporarily handled by Counselor Xiao Jirong.

Hurricane Warning

According to the Shanghai Observatory at 9 PM last night, the Zikawei Observatory issued a gale warning at 9 PM last night, stating that at 6 PM, a gale was located between 25.30 degrees north latitude and 126 degrees east longitude, with the center experiencing violent winds within 60 miles. It is moving northwest-west. The Central News Agency reported from Nanjing on the 25th that the hurricane approaching the south of Daito Island, according to the Central Meteorological Observatory, reached between Naba and Isisakyina Islands on the afternoon of the 25th, with strong winds moving northwest-west at a speed of 20 kilometers. Strong winds and rain have already occurred in the East China Sea and may approach the coastal areas of Wenzhou, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and northern Fujian within 24 hours, with winds intensifying.

Manchurian and Mongolian Woolen Fabrics Dumped in Shanghai, Taxed Only as Re-exported Domestic Goods, Half the Price of Imported Goods

The New News Agency reports that as the weather turns cooler, woolen fabrics are about to enter the market. It is reported that recently, a large batch of ABC serge woolen fabrics from the three northeastern provinces has arrived in Shanghai. The customs authorities call these woolen fabrics "Manchurian and Mongolian goods." They are originally produced in Shenyang and are taxed at only 7.5% as re-exported domestic goods, while imported woolen fabrics are taxed at over 55%, a significant difference. As a result, some people are even shipping Japanese woolen fabrics to the three northeastern provinces for repackaging before shipping them to Shanghai. It is reported that Ren Chang Woolen Fabrics has ordered more than 100 boxes from Yijing Foreign Firm, while Iwai and Abe City Foreign Firms have each ordered 60 boxes, with a value of over 200,000 taels.

The Central News Agency reports that Huang Fu, former Minister of the Interior, went to Mogan Mountain for convalescence. As the weather in Shanghai gradually cools, he descended the mountain and went to Hangzhou the morning before last.

Each industry inspection sub-committee should complete the inventory registration within this month. This notification is hereby recorded and issued. It is hoped that your association will promptly instruct its members and non-members to report their inventory and imports for registration in accordance with the inspection regulations and report their shipments for verification. The association should create a roster and report it to this chamber for verification. This is of utmost importance." Representative to the National Labor Congress, Zhu Xuefan, Arrived in Shanghai Last Night, Over 500 People from All Walks of Life Welcomed Him at the Port, Compiling a Report in Shanghai, Scheduled to Go to Nanjing on the 27th, Published a Speech on Attending the Congress and the Experience of the Inspection

The Ta Kung Pao reports that Zhu Xuefan, the labor representative of China appointed by the Central Government to attend the 20th International Labor Congress, arrived in Shanghai at 7 AM yesterday on the Italian postal ship Conte Verde. Representatives from all walks of life went to the port to welcome him. Banquets were held by various circles. The labor community is scheduled to convene a welcome rally. Mr. Zhu will compile a report in Shanghai and then proceed to Nanjing on the 27th to report the experience to the central authorities. The details are recorded below:

Welcoming Personnel

The representatives from all walks of life who went to the port to welcome him yesterday morning included Lu Jingshi of the Municipal Party Committee, Pan Gongzhan of the Social Affairs Bureau, Sun Lufing of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai Office, Guo Lanxin of the Shanghai-Wusong Garrison Headquarters, Zhang Yuliang of the Aviation Association, Cheng Haifeng of the China National Labor Bureau, Zhou Xuexiang, Shao Xubai, Li Mengnan, Long Peiyun, Ye Xianggao, Lu Muqin, and Gong Yuting of the General Labor Union, Zhao Shusheng of the China Labor Association, Zhang Kechang, Shui Xiangyun, Zhang Yidao, and Fan Caicong of the Postal Workers' Union, Tang Zhisheng, Wang Yusheng, and Yu Yongfu of the Heng Society, Xu Jianye of the Wharf Business Office, and various industry unions such as the Fourth District Cigarette, First District Water and Electricity, Automobile Drivers, Fourth District Loading and Unloading, Sixth District Water and Electricity, Tenth District Cotton Spinning, Newspaper, Tugboat, First District Cosmetics, and Brewing, as well as Huiling National Academy, Chen Jian, Lide, Minli, Zhimin, and Hualun and other schools, all colleagues of the newspaper, representatives of all circles, and friends of Mr. Zhu, totaling over 500 people.

Arrival Situation

The Italian ship Conte Verde entered the port at 5 AM yesterday morning and docked at the Qichang Wharf in Pudong. The welcoming representatives from all circles gathered at the New Customs Wharf from 5:30 AM onwards. The labor unions and schools all prepared banners welcoming "Mr. Zhu Xuefan's Return to China." In addition to the customs' launch, Heng Society, Postal Workers' Union, and Yi Society all boarded the Yuebao, Hongxin, and No. 5 municipal ferries to greet him. After Mr. Zhu shook hands with all the welcoming personnel on board, he transferred to the Yuebao ferry and arrived at the New Customs Wharf at 7:30 AM. Music was played and firecrackers were set off, creating a very lively atmosphere. Mr. Zhu then left the port and took a car back to his private residence on Huage Road to rest.

Mr. Zhu's Speech

Mr. Zhu gave a speech to the press corps on board, stating that he (Mr. Zhu referring to himself) was appointed to attend the 20th International Labor Congress. He specially raised the issues of (1) opium among overseas Chinese workers and (2) equal treatment of Chinese workers with international workers, which are currently crucial for China. The first case (opium issue) was jointly proposed with the French labor representative and was passed by the Congress. The second case (equal treatment) was also passed by the Congress, and a committee was formed to draft a convention, which will be formally included in the agenda for discussion at the 22nd Congress in 1938. In addition, the Congress passed a resolution to reduce the 48-hour work week to 40 hours. He reported to the Congress the rampant smuggling in North China, which endangers the national economy and people's livelihoods, and also received the press corps from various countries, explaining the loss of national tax revenue and the decline of industry and commerce in China due to smuggling. Although working hours are reduced, their work efficiency is stronger than that of Chinese workers. The educational level of workers is generally seven to nine years of national education. Labor insurance for workers in case of unemployment, accidental death, etc., is very developed. Workers in Italy and Germany have large-scale organizations for sports and entertainment. The government provides workers with various welfare facilities such as travel, which are very complete. After the Congress closed, he visited Italy, the United Kingdom, the Netherlands, France, Russia, and other countries to inspect the labor conditions and industries of various countries, each with its own strengths. The representatives of various countries gave him a warm reception, which he was very pleased with. He is very grateful for the welcome he received from all walks of life during his trip to Europe and his return to China.

Welcome from All Circles

The members of Heng Society in this city held a welcome banquet at Heng Society on Sapo Road at 12 PM yesterday. At 7 PM, Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau, hosted a dinner at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road to welcome Mr. Zhu. On the 28th of this month, Lu Jingshi of the Municipal Party Committee, Zhou Xuexiang, Standing Committee Member of the General Labor Union, and others will jointly host a banquet. At 12 PM on the 30th, more than 80 labor unions in this city will hold a welcome rally at the Atlantic Restaurant on Fourth Avenue and invite Mr. Zhu to report on the experience of attending the Congress. In addition, various public organizations will also hold separate welcome dinners.

Scheduled to Go to Nanjing

Mr. Zhu will rest briefly in Shanghai due to travel fatigue and compile a report on the experience of attending the 20th International Labor Congress. He is scheduled to take the night express train to Nanjing on the 27th of this month to report to the Ministry of Industry and other competent authorities on the experience of attending the Congress.

Tomorrow is Confucius' Birthday Commemoration, Representatives from All Walks of Life to Hold a Commemoration Meeting, The Entire City Will Have a Holiday and Hang Flags to Celebrate

Tomorrow (the 27th) is the anniversary of the birth of Confucius, the founder of Confucianism. This city, jointly convened by the Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Government, has scheduled representatives from all walks of life to hold a commemoration meeting at the Dacheng Hall of the Confucius Temple at 9 AM tomorrow. The presidium of the meeting will consist of seven agencies and organizations from the Party, government, military, agriculture, industry, commerce, and education. The Municipal Party Committee has appointed Committee Member Pan Gongzhan to serve as chairman. The commemoration meeting procedures and notices are recorded below:

Commemoration Procedures

(1) Convene a "Shanghai City Representatives from All Walks of Life Hold a Commemoration Meeting for the Birthday of Confucius"; (2) Date: August 27, 9 AM; (3) Venue: Dacheng Hall, Municipal Public Education Center, Confucius Temple Road; (4) Commemoration fee: jointly prepared by the Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Government; (5) Meeting Organization: Presidium consists of the Municipal Party Committee, the Municipal Government, the Garrison Headquarters, the Municipal Farmers' Association, the General Labor Union, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Municipal Education Association (6) Venue Decoration: Responsible by the Municipal Government; (7) Meeting Reception: Responsible by the Municipal Government, the masters of ceremonies, recorders, and ushers are responsible by the Municipal Party Committee; (8) From August 25, the Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Government jointly issued a notice: A. A holiday for one day for the commemoration day, hang flags to celebrate; B. All agencies, groups, schools, and all levels of party headquarters in this city shall send representatives with letters to participate; (9) Send a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to send police to maintain order at the meeting place and dispatch a military band to the meeting to play music (handled by the Municipal Government).

Notice of the Meeting

The Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Government issued a joint notice regarding the commemoration of Confucius' birthday, stating, "It is hereby notified that the 27th of this month is the nationally designated day for commemorating the birthday of Confucius. All circles will have a holiday for one day on this day and hang flags to celebrate. It is also scheduled to convene all circles to hold a commemoration meeting at the Dacheng Hall of the Municipal Public Education Center on Confucius Temple Road in the South City at 9 AM on the same day. A joint notification is hereby issued, hoping that all agencies, groups, schools, and all levels of party headquarters in this city will send two representatives on time with letters to participate as necessary. This is hereby notified."

Hang Flags and Take a Holiday

Tomorrow is Confucius' birthday commemoration. In addition to the Municipal Party Committee and the Municipal Government jointly convening all circles to hold a commemoration meeting, all agencies, groups, schools, all levels of party headquarters, factories, companies, and commercial firms in the city will have a holiday for one day and hang flags to celebrate. The police authorities in the Foreign Concession will implement security measures for this purpose.

The Ministry of Railways Reorganizes the Debts of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway, After Sincere Consultation with Bondholders, The Interest Rate Will Be Reduced to 2.5% Within 20 Years, And 4/5 of the Arrears Will Be Forgiven, The Principal Will Be Repaid Within 50 Years

The Central News Agency reports that the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway borrowed 1.5 million pounds from a British banking syndicate in the 33rd year of the Guangxu reign of the former Qing Dynasty. The railway was completed four years later. The main business was passenger transport, and freight transport only accounted for one-tenth. The route was short, and competition from shipping between Hong Kong and Guangdong was fierce. The railway's revenue was insufficient, and the repayment of principal and interest in previous years was subsidized by other railways. It had never been independently financed. Furthermore, the political situation in Guangdong Province was unstable, and no one paid attention to the debt. As a result, the principal and interest have been in arrears since June 1925, accumulating to a huge sum of over 1.55 million pounds. Now that the situation in Guangdong has stabilized, the central government, in order to maintain national credit, is responsible for reorganizing the Guangzhou-Kowloon loan. After sincere consultation with the bondholders, the bondholders were fortunately able to understand the difficult situation and cooperate sincerely. Regarding the interest rate, it will be reduced from 5% to 2.5% within 20 years, and 4/5 of the arrears will be forgiven. The principal will be repaid within 50 years. The Ministry of Railways is deeply grateful for the cooperation of the bondholders and is determined to renovate the railway administration to increase the railway revenue and implement the original intention of maintaining credit. The detailed measures were announced yesterday. The notice issued by the Minister of Railways yesterday regarding the measures to restore the 1905 bonds of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway is as follows: (1) From June 1, 1937, the bond interest will be paid at 2.5% per year for the first 20 years, and 5% will be paid thereafter. However, if the net revenue of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway exceeds 200,000 yuan in national currency in any year within the first 20 years, the excess amount should be used to increase the interest payment first, up to a maximum of 5%, and the remaining amount should be used to increase the principal repayment; (2) From June 1, 1936, 550,000 yuan in national currency will be prepared annually as a reserve fund for the repayment of principal and interest. Of this amount, 350,000 yuan will be allocated by the Ministry of Railways from its funds, and the remaining 200,000 yuan will be allocated by the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway Bureau. From June 1941, the Ministry of Railways will allocate an additional 250,000 yuan for principal repayment, increasing the total reserve fund to 800,000 yuan; (3) From June 1, 1937, the balance of the reserve fund, after deducting the interest payment, will be used for principal repayment. The principal of this loan shall be fully repaid within a maximum of 50 years; (4) 4/5 of the arrears will be canceled, and the remainder will be exchanged for non-interest-bearing small notes. The small notes will be repaid after the principal has been repaid. Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Railways stated that for the benefit of the Chinese government and the bondholders, he has already begun to improve the condition of the Guangzhou-Kowloon Railway and its management methods.

Freight Rates for Goods to the United States Will Increase Starting in September, Average Increase of 20%, Only Lake Silk Will Remain at the Old Rate

Since all shipping companies on the Pacific route have joined the Freight Conference, the freight rates for goods shipped from Shanghai to the United States (Honolulu, San Francisco, Los Angeles, Vancouver, Victoria, Tacoma, Seattle, and Portland) will be increased by the twelve shipping companies of the conference, including American Mail, Changxing, Dollar, Kawasaki, International, American President Lines (New York Line), NYK, Osaka, Pacific, and Yamashita Kisen. For goods shipped from the Yangtze River, Ningbo, Qingdao, Yantai, Weihaiwei, and Niuzhuang and exported from Shanghai, the freight rate, whether it is 40 cubic feet per ton or 2,000 pounds per ton, will be increased by an average of 20% from September 1, according to the original No. 6 "Delive." For example, the freight rate for mineral sand will increase from 8 yuan per ton to 10 yuan, the freight rate for soybeans (packaged) will increase from 7 yuan per ton to 8.5 yuan, the freight rate for porcelain will increase from 12 yuan per ton to 14 yuan, and the freight rate for tea will increase from 5 yuan per ton to 6 yuan. However, the freight rate for Lake silk will remain unchanged. The above freight rates are calculated in US dollars. The shipping companies have already notified the customers of the price increase.

National Postal Workers' General Union Continues to Strive for Participation in the National Election

The National Postal Workers' General Union is the general organization of postal worker groups in various regions and the highest leadership of postal employees nationwide. Its mission is to assist the authorities in developing postal services, improving the lives of workers, and enhancing mutual aid. It is also very active in patriotic actions and social undertakings. The organization is well-structured and firmly united, holding a significant position among workers' groups. In May of this year, the central government announced the National Assembly Representative Election Law, which did not include provisions for postal worker groups to elect representatives. The union, considering this a matter of postal workers' rights and interests, immediately submitted three proposals to the central government and the National Government for adoption. These proposals generally requested: (1) recognition of postal workers' right to participate in elections in the name of their group; (2) the formation of a separate electoral unit for postal workers to directly elect representatives; and (3) the allocation of representative quotas according to population proportions. Details were published in various newspapers at the time and will not be repeated here. The union, noting that special industry unions such as those for telegraph, railway, and maritime workers faced similar situations, jointly petitioned the central government in Beijing, striving for a unified solution. Subsequently, the railway and maritime unions were granted special permission by the central government to designate representatives within their local representative quotas. However, postal and telegraph representatives remained unassigned. Postal employees nationwide were quite perplexed by this decision and have repeatedly petitioned the union to firmly continue its efforts. Recently, the National Postal Workers' General Union submitted another petition to the Ministry of Public Training of the Central Government, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and the General Office for the Election of Representatives of the National Assembly, earnestly stating the reasons why postal workers should have the freedom of association and election, and urging them to accept and implement it. The original petition is recorded below: "Upon investigation, postal employees, due to the lack of provisions for representatives of postal worker groups in the National Assembly Representative Election Law, previously petitioned the Central National Government and the Executive and Legislative Yuans to add representative quotas, and jointly appealed with special industry unions such as postal, telegraph, railway, and shipping in Beijing. The responsible personnel of various agencies sympathized and accepted the petition, promising to devise remedial measures. Subsequently, the maritime and railway unions were allowed to designate representatives within their local representative quotas. However, no clear order has been issued for the postal and telegraph unions. Yesterday, we received a letter from the General Office for the Election of Representatives of the National Assembly stating that the National Postal Workers' General Union, the National Postal Workers' General Association, and local workers' unions are not legally founded and are not allowed to participate in the election. Upon reading this, the public was perplexed. In addition to sending a special letter to the General Office for the Election of Representatives of the National Assembly requesting clarification, we hereby respectfully present the reasons why postal personnel should have the freedom of association and election, hoping for your review and approval. Article 14 of the Provisional Constitution of the Republic of China during the Period of Political Tutelage states that people have the freedom of association and assembly, and shall not be suspended or restricted except in accordance with the law. Although postal personnel are civil servants, they are still citizens and should have no doubt about it. Therefore, they have the freedom to exercise the rights granted by the Provisional Constitution. The phrase "shall not be suspended or restricted except in accordance with the law" refers to situations where the nature of assembly and association endangers public order and morals, or there is a risk of endangering public order and morals, and the state laws have explicit provisions for suspension or restriction. The existing postal personnel organization was established in accordance with the policies of the Chinese Kuomintang, and for more than ten years, it has never deviated from the supervision and guidance of the party. Its purpose is pure and should not be subject to suspension or restriction. Past experience further confirms our confidence, which we believe is already well understood and does not require further elaboration. As for the General Office for the Election of Representatives of the National Assembly's letter stating that it is not legally founded, it must be because the postal worker groups have not been reorganized in accordance with the Postal Workers' Union Organization Regulations promulgated by the Executive Yuan of the National Government on October 5, 1932. However, Article 3 of the Trade Union Law states, 'Workers in national administrative, transportation, state-owned industries, educational institutions, public utilities, and various government agencies may use this law to organize trade unions, but their officials, employees, and workers of military and military industrial agencies are not included.' This effectively suspends the right of association for most postal personnel, which is in conflict with the spirit of the party platform and the Provisional Constitution. Moreover, the organizational rules of the postal workers' union

Statistics on National Textile Mill Cotton Production and Shutdowns in the First Half of the 25th Year

According to the Central News Agency, the China Cotton Mill Owners Association announced the following statistics on national textile mills for the first half of the 25th year: (1) cotton sales, (2) cotton inventory, and (3) shutdown status. (1) From January 1 to June 30 of this year, textile mills sold 1,155,347 bales of cotton (500 pounds per bale), a decrease of 29,886 bales compared to the second half of last year and a decrease of 17,803 bales compared to the same period last year. Among them, Chinese cotton accounted for 1,072,107 bales, an increase of 9,938 bales compared to the second half of last year and an increase of 80,234 bales compared to the first half of last year. American cotton accounted for 38,722 bales, a decrease of 30,724 bales compared to the second half of last year and a decrease of 64,989 bales compared to the first half of last year. Indian cotton accounted for 30,589 bales, a decrease of 8,707 bales compared to the second half of last year and a decrease of 25,816 bales compared to the first half of last year. Egyptian cotton accounted for 12,650 bales, an increase of 364 bales compared to the second half of last year and a decrease of 534 bales compared to the first half of last year. Other types of cotton accounted for 1,279 bales, also a decrease compared to last year. This is mainly due to exchange rate issues, which have made foreign cotton more expensive when converted, and heavy import taxes. Therefore, textile mills have gradually reduced their use of foreign cotton. (2) As of July 1, textile mills had an inventory of 392,127 bales of cotton, an increase of 33,251 bales compared to the second half of last year and an increase of 76,155 bales compared to the same period last year. Among them, the inventory of American and Chinese cotton was roughly similar to the second half of last year, but the inventory of Indian cotton increased by 19,390 bales. The reason for this is that last year's domestic cotton crop was poor, the supply of coarse cotton was insufficient, and market prices rose. In the spring, Indian cotton prices fell sharply, so some was imported to meet demand. However, most of it arrived in May and June, so the inventory of Indian cotton was higher at the end of June. (3) From January to June, the number of spindles shut down reached 1,555,014, an increase of 194,731 compared to the second half of last year. However, the average shutdown time decreased slightly. If calculated based on the total number of spindles nationwide, the number of weeks of shutdown was 5.06 weeks, similar to the second half of last year, but an increase of 1.34 weeks compared to the first half of last year. The increase in the shutdown rate indicates that the textile industry is still in a very difficult situation. Furthermore, it is based on this unsound trade union law that is being formulated, resulting in numerous flaws and even greater fragmentation. For example, it forcefully divides postal clerks and postal assistants into officials and workers. For postal employees with equal duties and the same appointments, one is considered ineligible to form a trade union, while the other is considered eligible. This is inconsistency number one. Furthermore, the law stipulates that the organizational members of postal workers' unions are limited to postal assistants, postal carriers, and mail carriers. However, the existing postal workers' associations and postal workers' unions actually include postal clerks. This type of organization has been the case from the beginning and cannot be easily changed. National legislation should be based on the social background, because the social background has the power to influence the law, and the law cannot change society. Moreover, in recent legislative practices in various countries, the right of association for civil servants is recognized. For example, the Lloyd-La Follette Act of 1912 in the United States, the labor law and draft new constitution of Soviet Russia, the German federal constitution, and the constitution of the Free City of Danzig all clearly stipulate that civil servants have the freedom of association. Our country's legislation has always been known for adopting the latest legislative examples, but it has disregarded the right of association for civil servants, which not only has the suspicion of obliterating facts but also misses the opportunity to take advantage of the situation. This is inconsistency number two. In summary, the organization of postal personnel has historical and social roots. The reason why it cannot be reorganized according to law is due to the inadequacy of the law, not the postal personnel's disregard for laws and regulations. We believe that the right to vote is the most important of the four rights and is a stepping stone to implementing constitutional government, which is of great importance. All citizens have the right to exercise it according to law, and postal personnel, as citizens, are no exception. Moreover, they are numerous and spread throughout the country, and their profession is a unified national transportation and political necessity. Therefore, postal personnel are particularly important to the election administration. Now that the election of representatives to the National Assembly is about to begin, the organizational issues have suddenly forced postal personnel to be unable to participate in the election in the name of their group. Not to mention the concern of postal personnel for national affairs, even those who bear the heavy responsibility of the party and the country will not know how to explain themselves. The timing is urgent. For the sake of their own rights and interests and for the sake of the constitutional government, postal personnel have no choice but to implore the Central National Government to adopt the legislative precedents of various countries, as well as the spirit of the country's provisional constitution and party platform, and to re-examine and revise the existing trade union law and the postal workers' union organization regulations, so that postal worker groups have a legal basis and the central government can fulfill its leadership responsibilities. Before the aforementioned laws and regulations can be revised, in order to enable postal worker groups to participate in the election of national representatives, please immediately devise remedial measures, allow participation in trade union elections, and avoid any shortcomings in the constitutional project. This is a pressing request, and we sincerely hope that you will review and promptly handle it, and we will be deeply grateful."

Rice and Wheat Prices Are Low; Domestic Rice Can Be Shipped to Guangdong

This year, most parts of our country have reported good harvests, but due to Japanese merchants buying up rice, wheat, and miscellaneous grains in large quantities, prices have soared. Although the authorities have imposed restrictions, the rising trend is still difficult to curb. According to sources in the grain trade, Japanese merchants have recently stopped buying in the north, and manufacturers have also shown little interest due to the high price of wheat, so wheat prices have suddenly fallen. As for rice prices, they are also trending lower as new crops enter the market. It is also understood that after the Guangdong incident is resolved, the import of foreign rice will be handled according to import tariffs, so the import of foreign rice into Guangdong will likely decrease, and domestic rice can be shipped to Guangdong for sale.

National Election Representatives from the Legal Profession to Be Allocated Among Three Regions

The Lawyers Association of the Republic of China held its second executive committee meeting in Qingdao. In addition to the attending executive committee members, there were also more than 50 people, including the association's secretary-general, various secretaries, and the various secretaries of the Wrongful Imprisonment Compensation Movement Committee, to discuss various cases. In addition to matters related to judicial reform, the most important issue was the election of representatives to the National Assembly. Because there are more than 80 lawyers' associations across the country, and the quota for representatives to the National Assembly is only set at ten, it is difficult to allocate the seats due to the limited number of seats and the large number of applicants. The attending committee members took this opportunity to exchange views and reached a satisfactory result. The pre-determined allocation of representative quotas will be divided into three regions: (1) South China Region, including the lawyer's associations of the capital, Shanghai, Hangzhou, and Guangzhou, the region with the most members, is allocated seven seats; (2) North China Region, including the lawyer's associations of Beijing, Tianjin, Shandong, etc., the region with the second largest number of members, is allocated five seats; (3) Central China Region, including the lawyer's associations of Sichuan, Hankou, Jiangxi, and other provinces, because they have the fewest members, voluntarily withdrew. Among the above-mentioned twelve people, ten representatives from the legal profession will be elected in the final election.

Intestine Industry Association Petitions Ministry of Finance to Stop Two Factories from Taking Advantage

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Intestine Industry Association previously submitted a document to the Ministry of Finance, stating: "This is a petition for the matter. It is stated in the letter from the association's member, China Intestine Factory, etc., that a non-member fellow trader, Chengda Intestine Factory (factory address is on Deswei Road, Hongkou, Shanghai; manager is Cheng Zhongxin), has been manufacturing pig intestines for export for many years. Suddenly, in February of last year, they came up with a novel idea: they concentrated the pig intestines from various ports in Shanghai and transported them to Zhoushan, Zhejiang, to set up a factory for manufacturing. After the work was completed, they transported them back to Shanghai. Upon investigation, Zhoushan is a salt production area, where salt is only worth about two yuan per dan. Now, in Shanghai, it is ten yuan and six jiao per dan per hundred market catties, more than five times the price of salt in Zhoushan. This is why they took this action. Upon investigation, the manufacture of pig intestines requires about 400 catties of salt per barrel. Assuming one barrel per day, the advantage they are taking is considerable. Then, in March of this year, another non-member, Hanli Intestine Factory (factory address is on Beijing Jiang Road, Zha Bei, Shanghai; manager is Wu Lihou), also set up a branch factory in Zhoushan and intensified their actions, smuggling private salt into Shanghai. The salt can then be used to make pig intestines in their Shanghai factory. The extent of taking advantage of the law and the scope is more than ten times that of Chengda Factory. Since Hanli Factory has such illegitimate benefits, their costs must be reduced. Therefore, their sales are successful, and fellow traders are harmed. As a result, 70-80% of them have stopped production. Those who plan to follow suit and move to Zhoushan to set up factories are endless. Hanli Factory only cares about its own selfishness and does not consider the national tax revenue. Members, etc., cannot bear the long-term harm to national tax revenue and the interests of fellow traders, so they specifically ask your association to forward this to the competent authorities to find ways to stop it in order to protect the safety of fellow traders, etc., to the association. Based on this, the state's tax revenue, especially salt, is very important. The Hanli Chengda factories are taking advantage and daring to use the transportation of goods to leak private salt. Shanghai is not the only industry that needs salt to manufacture goods. If various soy sauce gardens, etc., follow suit, what will the future of national tax revenue be? If those who use salt to make goods nationwide follow suit and move to salt-producing areas, the national tax revenue will be unimaginable. The association has sent personnel to investigate and confirm that this is the case. It is appropriate to prepare a document and submit it to the department to quickly stop it in order to deter others, which is in the public interest. Sincerely submitted."

British Cruiser: A Deserter Captured: Remains Hidden in Shanghai After Desertion for Sixteen Months

The Shanghai Times reports that on April 14th of last year, a common sailor named Harris, only 20 years old, deserted from the British cruiser HMS Suffolk, which was docked in the Huangpu River. Despite extensive searches by the British naval authorities, his whereabouts were unknown. After deserting, the sailor used the alias Wei Bai and remained in Shanghai. In July of this year, probably because he was tired of the life of hiding and regretting his past mistakes, he wrote to the British Admiralty, appealing for forgiveness. In his letter, he indicated a Shanghai address where a reply could be sent and received. Based on this address, the British naval authorities in Shanghai issued an arrest warrant and sent it to the Shanghai Municipal Police. The police dispatched Western detective Bai Latlai to arrest the suspect. Based on the address in the letter, Bai searched in the Hongkou district for a long time and finally arrested the suspect on Monday morning. According to his confession, he deserted from the ship because he was not used to the discipline of the navy. For the past sixteen months, he has been making a living teaching English at a Chinese school in Hongkou and living in that district. The police have now escorted the suspect to the British ship HMS Thistle, which is moored in the Huangpu River, where he is being temporarily detained pending court-martial. It is reported that Harris has served in the navy for four years and is from London, where his mother currently lives.

The Xin Sheng News Agency reports that the hotel industry in this city believes that the New Life Movement's implementation measures to suppress extra tips, stipulating that security deposits for workers are not allowed, replaced by shop guarantees, and that workers' wages should be determined, while tips voluntarily given by customers will be turned over to be used as aviation donations, pose a major threat to the business. It has already submitted a request to the party and government organs, recounting various difficulties and requesting a modification. A reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency visited the person in charge of the Hotel Industry Association yesterday and received a detailed account of the current business situation of the hotel industry and the process of testing the opinions of the workers on this case. The details are recorded as follows:

Business Conditions

The person in charge stated that the hotel industry's business was still good before the January 28th Incident. Since the post-war destruction of the city, coupled with the frequent disasters in the interior, all industries have felt the economic downturn. With fewer merchants traveling back and forth, the hotel industry has plummeted. Now, more than 600 large and small businesses in the city are all deeply wounded and feel unable to maintain themselves. Although they have lowered prices to attract customers, many rooms are still vacant. If they now follow the regulations of the New Life Movement, they must not only provide security deposits but also suddenly increase wages, then the general trend will inevitably lead to bankruptcy. This is not alarmist; it is a fact that is obvious to all. According to the New Life Movement's regulations, fixed wages will be used and the extra tips will be transferred to aviation donations. The association conducted a test of the absolute majority of the workers, all of whom expressed that they could not agree. This is because the workers can earn 20 or 30 yuan in tips voluntarily given by customers during peak months. If the management is forced to stipulate wages, the standard wages will inevitably be very low and difficult for the workers to accept.

Test Opinions

In order to test the opinions of the workers, the association issued a notice to all businesses a few days ago, stating that in order to suppress extra tips, the New Life Movement Promotion Association first needs to establish workers' wages. The association believes that the following method is of the greatest concern to the industry. What are the opinions of the workers employed by each business? A comprehensive investigation is urgently needed to understand the true intentions of all workers and to determine the policy that the industry should adopt. Therefore, a test survey form is issued, hoping to be forwarded to each worker. The worker who is willing to accept which method should sign his name in his own handwriting under which method. It should be sent to the association immediately for verification. This is a special notice.
