Detectives and Bandits: Fierce Battle in Western Shanghai: Both Sides Opened Fire Thirty to Forty Times; Three Passersby Injured, One Bandit Captured

At 7:30 last night, four bandits, each armed with guns, suddenly arrived at the residence of the manager of a large department store at No. 19, Lusena Road. They broke into the inner room and searched wantonly. At that time, the owner and servants of the house, seeing that things were not good, immediately reported the crime to the police station. The Jing'an Temple police station in charge received the news and immediately dispatched a large number of armed detectives to rush to encircle and arrest them. However, the bandits were unusually alert and silently observed that the behavior of the owner and others was not right, and they immediately took the stolen goods and fled out the door to the west. Unexpectedly, they met the detectives. The bandits fled towards Daxilu Road, firing shots to resist arrest along the way. All the detectives also chased and fired back. When they reached the intersection of Daxilu and Dunxin Road, the bandits saw that the detectives had gathered from all sides and could not escape. They immediately leaned against the wall and confronted the police. Then, a fierce battle began between the two sides. In total, no less than thirty to forty bullets were fired, as dense as a string of beads, and bullets fell like rain. At this time, a bandit hoped to escape from Dunxin Road and was arrested by a detective. The remaining three bandits waited until the bullets were exhausted and then fled into the dark wilderness there. Because they were released by the rabbit, only when the detectives were engaged in fierce fighting did two women and a rickshaw puller get injured by stray bullets. One was the wife of Cai Chunyuan, a comprador at a Westerner's house at No. 27 Dunxin Road, 26 years old, who was hit in the left eye by a bullet that exited from the back of her head, and her condition was extremely critical. One was an old woman from Jiangbei in a thatched shed there, about 50 years old, who was injured in the right ear. The rickshaw puller was only injured in the leg and was not seriously injured. All were sent to the hospital for treatment by the detectives. A bandit was captured alive and taken to the police station for detention, pending the arrest of his accomplices and joint investigation.

Inside A Teahouse in Caoxiebang, A Bloodied Man; Chopped Five Times with an Axe While Having Tea; Police Have Captured Two Criminals

Last night at 8 o'clock, the Public Concession Putuo Road Police Station suddenly received a post alarm, stating that a murder case had occurred in a teahouse in Caoxiebang, and the murderers had all fled. The police station received the news and immediately dispatched detectives to rush there. They only saw a man lying in the teahouse, covered in blood, about 20 years old, wearing white broadcloth pants, barely breathing. They quickly summoned an ambulance and rushed him to the hospital for treatment. It was found that the man had been chopped 15 times with an axe, with the most serious injury in the waist. He was completely unable to speak, so his name was unknown. Observing his appearance, he looked like a vagrant. According to people in the teahouse, the cause of the victim was caused by qi jiang cha (gangland mediation). As for the appearance of the murderer, some were also slightly familiar. The police then arrested two murderers in the vicinity based on this point and learned that there were still accomplices, who are currently under strict investigation. However, the injured person suffered severe injuries and was on the verge of death. It was heard that he had died of his injuries by 12 o'clock, ordering the Joint Association of New Pharmaceutical Industry Guilds of the City, presenting a case for requesting the speedy formulation of measures for the transportation and sale of medicinal quinine, saccharin, lactose, and gelatin powder, in order to alleviate the difficulties of merchants. Having been informed, it is found that the Administrative Yuan's 272nd Yuan Yi [meeting] has decided that there is no need to restrict or ban the transportation and sale of saccharin, sugar powder, and lactose in order to benefit the proper use of the medical industry. According to the previous situation, the relevant documents of the case will be copied and ordered to be informed. However, saccharin and other items can indeed be mixed into heroin, red and white pills, etc., to increase the weight of drugs. If pharmaceutical merchants and colleagues properly transport and sell these items for proper medical use, they must sell them with caution. If the anti-smoking authorities conduct inspections, they should at any time accurately indicate the sales channels for verification. This order includes a copy of a public letter from the Administrative Yuan, a copy of a public letter originally attached from the Ministry of Health, and a copy of the minutes of the review meeting. The Main Culprit in the Case of Beating a Laborer to Death Has Been Arrested; Verified that Death Was Due to Spleen Injury Turning into Disease

At about 4 o'clock in the afternoon of the 20th of this month, Western Constable No. 252 of the Old Gate Police Station, while patrolling the intersection of Suzhou Road and Fujian Road, saw a man lying on the side of the road. He immediately called an ambulance to come and send him to Renji Hospital for diagnosis and treatment. On one hand, he reported back to the police station, and under investigation by Chinese Detective Yan Shiqing, it was learned that the man's name was Liu Hailin, 21 years old, from Wuxi. After being diagnosed by the doctor, Liu's spleen was severely injured. At the time, because Liu was unconscious, he did not know the cause of the injury. Yan went to the scene to investigate. According to the merchants in the vicinity, several laborers from the Public Works Department of the Ministry of Industry had a conflict with a worker-like person while washing and sweeping the streets in the Suzhou Fujian Road area. They beat each other, and the worker fell to the ground. The laborers of the Public Works Department also dispersed. Detective Yan went to the Public Works Department to investigate. It turned out that the workers had been dispatched to the area at that time. He then ordered all the workers to go to Shiji Hospital to let Liu Hailin identify them. Liu pointed out worker Li Shengnian No. 163 among the workers. The detective then detained Li. Li confessed that the person who beat Liu was actually Shen Guisheng, a laborer No. 155. It was found that Shen Guisheng had not arrived at the scene when he was identified at Renji Hospital, and that Liu Changgui had replaced him, which was obviously false. Shen was arrested in a thatched shed on Gonghe New Road on the day before yesterday and brought to the Public Security Bureau. Shen confessed that he had beaten Liu. The detectives requested that Shen be brought back first to allow Liu to identify him, but the Public Security Bureau did not allow it. By the time he was brought back, Liu had already died at 3 p.m. the day before yesterday, so it was too late. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Special First Court. The police lawyer Wang Yaotang prosecuted him according to Article 258, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law, for injury causing death. When Shen was questioned, he confessed that he had beaten the deceased in the buttocks, but Liu had acted first. Judge Qian Hongye then ordered a postponement of one week for further interrogation. Subsequently, Inspector Tang of the Special First Court arrived at the corpse site to examine it. It was verified that Liu Hailin had indeed suffered a spleen injury before his death, had undergone surgery, and had died from a disease. The corpse was handed over to the Pushan Villa for burial.

New Pharmaceutical Industry Representative Went to Beijing and Zhenjiang Yesterday to Petition for the Debt of Two Pharmacies in Wuxi

Zhu Yuquan, Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association, Yuan Hesong, Supervisory Committee Member, and others, went to Beijing and Zhenjiang yesterday with a written petition. The petition stated: "Submitting this document is regarding the Wuxi Taihe and Zhongwai Pharmacies, which are suspected of drug trafficking. Their assets have been completely confiscated, affecting creditors and hindering the execution of civil trials. We request a review and instructions on relief measures. The petitioners are the creditors of the Wuxi Taihe and Zhongwai Pharmacies, totaling seventy-nine households (organized as a group). The total amount of debt under Taihe's name is 32,458 yuan, 9 jiao, 3 fen, and 5 li. The total amount of debt under Zhongwai's name is 31,961 yuan, 7 jiao, and 9 fen, and 7 li. All are legitimate commercial debts. It is inappropriate that the Taihe Pharmacy was ordered to be sealed by the local government due to suspected drug trafficking. Furthermore, because Hu Shutang, the owner of Zhongwai Pharmacy, is one of the shareholders of Taihe Pharmacy, Zhongwai Pharmacy was also subjected to the same sealing treatment. After hearing the news, the petitioners believed that the business's assets were the entire guarantee for all its external debts. They repeatedly submitted petitions and sent representatives to the Second District Security Command of Jiangsu Province to state their reasons and request relief. In addition to receiving approval to wait for legal processing, they also discussed face-to-face to ensure that creditors would not suffer losses. The petitioners immediately filed lawsuits against Taihe and Zhongwai Pharmacies in accordance with the law, seeking payment. Subsequently, the Wuxi District Court issued judgments No. 204 and No. 205 in the 24th year, ordering Taihe and Zhongwai Pharmacies to repay the goods in full, which were finalized on record. After applying for enforcement, the Wuxi District Court inquired with the Second District Security Command of Jiangsu Province and planned to take over the sealed assets of the two pharmacies for valuation and auction. The reply stated, in essence, that Hu Shutang, who opened the Taihe Pharmacy, had been proven to have sold drugs, and all of his assets had been confiscated in accordance with the drug control and punishment regulations, and the case had been submitted for review. Hu Shutang has absconded and is being wanted. Before he is apprehended, there are doubts about the debts of the petitioners, and it was not approved. The petitioners were shocked after being informed of the situation by the Civil Enforcement Office of the Wuxi District Court. According to the recent interpretation by the Military Affairs Commission, the confiscation under the drug control and punishment regulations is limited to those who have no rights other than the offender. The Taihe and Zhongwai Pharmacies owe the petitioners tens of thousands of yuan. The majority of their assets, including drug inventory, were obtained from the petitioners without payment. Externally, these assets serve as the entire guarantee for their debts. Confiscating all of these assets at once would significantly harm the rights of the petitioners. Article 19 of the Provisional Regulations for Drug Control and Punishment, promulgated by the National Government on June 3 of this year, states that those who commit the crimes in Articles 3 to 5 of these regulations may have all or part of their property confiscated. The execution of property confiscation shall apply the provisions of the rules of civil procedure and the supplementary civil enforcement measures. There are two points that can be studied here. First, the nature of confiscation is an accessory punishment that must be declared simultaneously with the principal punishment after the offender is apprehended and tried. Whether or not confiscation should be imposed is based on the principle of discretion, and there is room for discretion. Second, since the execution of confiscation should apply the rules of civil enforcement law, any creditor who has obtained an enforcement title should not be excluded due to the confiscation. Currently, Hu Shutang, who is accused of drug trafficking, is still at large and has not been apprehended. The judgment or disposition of confiscating all of his assets should not be made in advance. Furthermore, the petitioners' debts have been finalized by judgment, they have obtained an enforcement title, and compulsory enforcement has begun. They should not be excluded due to suspicion. The Second District Security Command has obstructed the execution of the final civil judgment against Taihe and Zhongwai Pharmacies based on the confiscation of all of Hu Shutang's assets. Their view is undoubtedly mistaken. Therefore, we petition your honorable office to examine the previous situation, rectify the errors when reviewing the judgment of the case, and immediately provide relief measures so that the effectiveness of the court's judgment will not be hindered by drug control measures, and creditors will not suffer unexpected losses. This would be a great benefit. Respectfully submitted to the Jiangsu Security Command and the General Supervisor of Anti-Smoking of the Military Affairs Commission."

Huang Lijuan Sues Kong Zuan for Seduction and Abandonment; Civil Lawsuit Settled Out of Court; Criminal Lawsuit Concluded and Scheduled for Sentencing

Shen Bao National Goods Special Issue

Humble Suggestions to National Goods Female Interviewers

— Qiulang

Recently, the Shanghai Women's Association not only organized a women's national goods consumption group, but also held national goods home visits, inviting female interviewers to visit and persuade families to use national goods. I strongly agree with this initiative, as it is a good method and intention—because women are the rulers of the family, and all items used for food and clothing in the family are managed by the housewife. Now, using women as interviewers to visit and persuade housewives door-to-door will surely achieve significant results in the promotion of national goods and achieve twice the result with half the effort. The reason is that interviewers and housewives are of the same sex, which will make conversations more convenient. If they can earnestly persuade and advise, they can gain trust and understanding, which is very different from men persuading women, which is incompatible. However, I have two points to contribute to the female interviewers, and I will write them down below for adoption:

First, the age of the female interviewers should be middle-aged women, because if they are too young, people will think they are inexperienced and even ridicule them, and if they are too old, they will think they are outdated. As for their words, they should be tactful and alert, earnestly informing them of the advantages and disadvantages, so that listeners will be moved and naturally develop patriotic thoughts, and fulfill the responsibility of visiting and persuading.

Second, the female interviewers should wear badges on their chests to facilitate their entry into the boudoir and carefully inspect all the items in the room. Even if all the appliances or food in the room are imported goods or a large number of smuggled goods, they should calmly persuade them to eat and use up the existing ones, and not allow them to buy them again to avoid punishment. At the same time, they must also guide them to purchase high-quality national goods that can be substituted, so that people will not mistakenly purchase them. They must avoid speaking loudly and angrily, and becoming embarrassed and angry, which will cause resentment!

Other aspects of the female interviewers' own clothing and behavior should be strictly self-checked in advance! Do they adhere to the national goods creed without any conflicts? Because only by setting an example can they influence others.

Ladies Are Joining the Women's National Goods Consumption Association

— Yang'an

In this day and age, national goods are really having good luck. The East advocates national goods, and the West also advocates national goods. Especially the women's community is even more happy to participate in this national goods movement to save the country. The Shanghai Women's Association has organized a Women's National Goods Consumption Committee and is working hard to promote national goods. Recently, the Shanghai Municipal National Goods Movement Federation also sent letters to the managers of national goods factories and national goods companies, urging their wives to join the newly organized Women's National Goods Consumption Association. It is extremely meaningful and valuable for the family members of the leaders of the national goods industry to lead this national goods consumption work. I think that these wives of the leaders of the national goods industry are all known in society for being good helpmates. They usually help their husbands and do a lot of work. Now they also want to help their husbands to do the work of promoting national goods. Originally, the husband devoted himself to the national goods business all day long, and won many honors for national goods. Therefore, the wife should follow her husband to work hard to consume national goods. There is absolutely no situation in the world where the husband manufactures national goods, but the wife is happy to promote foreign goods. Therefore, it is a matter of course, the most reasonable, and the most practical and effective thing for the wives of the leaders of the national goods industry to promote national goods, sell national goods, and consume national goods. Without waiting for the husband to urge them to join, I think that the general wives will automatically and happily join, so that the loving couple can work together under the banner of the national goods movement.

We also want to go one step further. It is not enough for the wives to join the Women's National Goods Consumption Association. If they do not join, then so be it. After joining, they must earnestly implement it. When buying an item or using a utensil, they must first silently think about whether it is a Chinese product? Is it a genuine national product? The inspection must be serious, and the investigation must be strict. Not only must they be sincere to themselves, but they must also persuade relatives and encourage family members to work hard under the banner of national goods consumption. Do not be afraid of speaking until your tongue is tired and your lips are dry, do not be afraid of trouble, and even less be afraid of being disliked or ridiculed by others. Undoubtedly, resolutely and decisively work with your beloved husband to do this valuable national goods movement. The day when national goods are popular and foreign goods disappear is the day when the wives' merits are completed.

Reflections After Reading "The Position of National Goods in the National Economy"

— Meng Zhao

The national goods speech movement is indeed an urgent matter in this extraordinary period! It makes the Chinese people hear and understand the meaning of national goods broadcasting, and they can never forget it with every meal, deeply rooted in the hearts of the people! Its effect is very great! After reading Mr. Yang Yao's speech manuscript, "The Position of National Goods in the National Economy," I couldn't help but sigh.

People in the same industry must be jealous! This seems to be a unique iron law of China? Especially in the national goods business, instead of thinking about contacting and uniting, working together to improve, they only know jealousy! Imitation, destruction, and slander, so that mutual attacks are often heard. May I ask, if the national goods industry is internally scattered, what hope is there for the future of the business? It only reduces the compatriots' faith in using national goods! And national goods and the national economy will never have the hope of connection. This is one reason.

To seek the active development of national goods, studying the psychological preferences of the Chinese people is indeed the key! If national goods cater to the psychology of the Chinese people and are welcomed! Then the national goods psychological construction of the Chinese people is really the greatest force! As Mr. Pan said: "The major problem of my country's national goods lies in closing the door to build cars, in selfishness, and not catering to the psychology of general users, so that all products are not suitable for sale in various places..." These words are correct. From this point of view, it is difficult to win without studying the psychology of users. This is the second reason.

General merchants should also reflect! As Chinese, they should sell Chinese goods! They must not be accomplices! They must not be salesmen for foreign goods! They must not dig the grave of their own economic demise! This is the third reason.

Consumers should know to love and use national goods. The money is still flowing into the hands of the Chinese people. It is originally unnecessary to consider Chu bow Chu de. Instead, they should reform the ignorant and inferior psychology of using foreign goods as fashionable! Everyone knows this meaning, and then everyone will love and use national goods, learn the integrity of the people of strong countries everywhere, the country will not prosper, and the family will not flourish! And the position of the national economy will naturally be prosperous and consolidated! This is the fourth reason.

The rule of not purchasing and using national goods and not approving expenditure reimbursement should not only apply to government agencies, but also to general industrial, commercial, educational, and other agencies. If the general affairs office purchases goods and finds no valid national goods invoice, they should not be reimbursed. According to this method, they can change their course and honestly purchase national goods in the future! This is the fifth reason.

The above points are the opinions and thoughts that I have after reading Mr. Yang'an's speech manuscript!

Autumn and National Goods

— Wei Sigeng

The four seasons of the year are in constant cycle, and people have gone through the mild spring and the hot summer, and now it is the cool autumn.

Autumn is cool, and following autumn is the cold winter. However, although the seasons change like this, people's patriotic hearts must not be like the seasons, becoming cold and bleak! Becoming ruthless! It should always maintain the same level of warmth.

Therefore, since we already knew to use national goods in summer, we still have to use national goods in autumn, such as clothing, socks, shoes, and hats... These items that must be added when the seasons change, of course, still adhere to the previous principle: "Only national goods are used."

Also, in autumn, mosquitoes will spread malaria! And people who have eaten too much melon and fruit in the summer are prone to dysentery... All of these must be prevented and treated. I will also take this opportunity to introduce the giant branch mosquito coil from Wuzhou Pharmacy and the domestically produced dysentery treatment, "An Li Sheng."

Two Major National Woolen Fabrics Enter the Market

Empress Brand Glossy Wool · Double Hands Double Sheep Brand Wool

Woolen fabrics are mostly imported from abroad, with an annual outflow of more than ten million yuan. Since last year, prominent merchants Mr. Chen and Mr. Bi traveled east to study the wool weaving industry. After returning to China, they purchased a large number of machines and established the China Woolen Fabric Factory on Linqing Road, Yangshupu, employing thousands of workers. They meticulously produce Empress Brand four-strand cashmere glossy wool, with bright colors that do not fade in water, and the size is extra long. To make an underwear, if using foreign woolen fabric, it would require about two pounds, but if using Empress Brand glossy wool, one pound is more than enough. With the same price per pound each month, it is equivalent to buying two pounds of foreign goods with one pound of Empress Brand glossy wool. The lightness and softness of the texture are especially rare. Now that autumn and winter are approaching, a large batch has been rushed to market, and various places both domestic and foreign have been vying to purchase in bulk.

Yumin Woolen Fabric Company was established by Mr. Ni Xifang and others, a prominent figure in the wool yarn industry on Xingsheng Street. The woolen fabrics produced include the Double Hands Brand and the Double Sheep Brand. Mr. Ni has served in the woolen fabric industry for decades, with rich experience. He has unique insights into selecting raw materials and dyeing. Therefore, since its introduction last year, it has been popular for a time. Schoolgirls and ladies in boudoirs have been vying to buy it, and it is praised as a leader among national woolen fabrics. Starting this year, large quantities have been sent to various places, so there will be no worry of shortages as in previous years.

Education News

The General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts Holds National Boy Scout Work Exhibition Scheduled to Open in Nanjing on October 1st Sends Telegrams to Various Provinces and Cities Soliciting Boy Scout Products

The General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts, in order to encourage the automatic operation and exchange of knowledge of boy scouts throughout the country, to increase knowledge and insights, and to examine the actual situation of boy scout activities in various places, has decided to hold a national boy scout work exhibition in Beijing on October 1st of this year, so that boy scouts throughout the country can inspect it in Beijing, in order to learn from each other. Recently, it specially sent a telegram to the Municipal Education Bureau to instruct all schools under its jurisdiction that have already established boy scout groups to earnestly handle the matter. The micro-item method is recorded as follows:

(1) Types of micro-items: A. Boy Scout camp engineering model, B. Boy Scout tent and supplies model, C. Totem design, D. Natural specimens, E. Boy Scout activity photos, F. Various commemorative badges, G. Boy Scout drawings, H. Handicrafts, I. Embroidered fabrics, J. Chemical products, K. Carvings, L. National defense product models, M. Boy Scout administrative charts, N. Local products, O. Boy Scout outdoor life texts, P. Other Boy Scout works. (2) Solicitation period: From the date of receiving the solicitation notice until September 20th of this year. (3) Number of micro-items: Local councils and groups must submit more than five items each. (4) Exhibition period: From October 1st of the 25th year for a period of one month. (5) Solicitation labels: All products must be accompanied by a work label, using ink to indicate the purpose of the work and the production sequence in the style, and should be recorded in detail. (6) Awards: After the work exhibition, experts will be hired to evaluate the grade and give appropriate awards, and commemorative medals will be awarded. (7) Exhibition Location: General Association of Chinese Boy Scouts. (Note) (1) The work should be completely self-made as the criterion. (2) The work materials should be purely national goods. (3) Works of greater value that need to be retained can be compensated at a reasonable price. (4) The transportation costs for returning items will be borne by the Association. (5) When the work is sent to the Association, the label must be attached and submitted together.

The Future Trend of Social Education in Our Country and Its Improvement Training Film and Broadcasting Education Personnel Hasten to Compile Civil School Textbooks and Supplementary Readers

In the past 24 years, the central social education funding was only more than 809,000 yuan, accounting for only 2.3% of the total national education and cultural expenses. However, only 9 provinces and cities could raise social education funds that accounted for 10% to 20% of the total education expenses. In view of this, the Ministry of Education actively promoted social education in the 25th year. On the one hand, it allocated 1.1 million yuan from the temporary education construction fee in the central 25th year budget for public education, film and broadcasting education, etc. (500,000 for the public, 250,000 for films, 250,000 for broadcasting, and 100,000 for reading materials). On the other hand, it ordered the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities to refer to the repeated orders of the Ministry to raise social education funds, striving to gradually reach the standards set by the Ministry. Regarding the school-style public schools education, the provinces and cities have been ordered to expand as much as possible, but non-school-style, more popular and most common film and broadcasting education can deeply affect the people and widely spread. Therefore, the Ministry of Education organized film and broadcasting education committees this year, and the two associations jointly formed an electrical education personnel training class to train wireless radio technicians and educational film projection personnel for various provincial and municipal education institutions, for the use of implementing electrical education in various provinces and cities. This kind of training class is scheduled to start on September 10th. This is to cultivate social education teachers for the promotion of social education in the future. It is also a new tool for the Ministry of Education to use electrical education as an auxiliary tool for social education this year. As for the editing of public reading materials, it is also an essential task. During this difficult period, promoting public education is not only about teaching literacy. It is necessary to awaken national consciousness and infuse patriotic thoughts. Therefore, improving public textbooks and compiling supplementary readers is an essential plan. It is heard that the Ministry of Education has begun to edit and improve public reading materials. Generally, for public school textbooks, carefully selected teaching materials for civics, national language, common sense, and music are mixed and compiled, with nationalism as the ideological center. It has begun editing, aiming to distribute them to various provinces and cities for application before the start of the next semester. After the textbooks are compiled, teaching methods will be rushed to meet the needs. The advanced textbooks will be started in the spring. All current public school textbooks will be reviewed, and the excellent ones will be rewarded. Those that are unsuitable will be ordered to be revised or banned. In addition, supplementary textbooks for public schools are planned to be compiled by experts according to local conditions, including one book for farmers, workers, businessmen, and women, and one each for the central, northern, and southern regions, according to climate and soil conditions. After the public school textbooks are completed, the editing will continue. For public supplementary reading materials, the biggest task is to edit the public library, which aims to develop national consciousness, cultivate national morality, supplement common sense of life, facilitate self-study in spare time, and guide the nation's self-awareness and upward movement. The editing method is divided into social, natural, application, self-cultivation, and national construction historical materials and party doctrines. The second is to edit comic strips, because those that are already popular in the market mostly contain obscenity, theft, and the promotion of gods and monsters and superstition. Therefore, efforts are made to remedy them and compile new versions to replace them. The third is to edit other popular reading materials, public dictionaries, study basic characters and basic words for the public, and improve various current public supplementary reading materials. These are all the general situations of the Ministry of Education's careful sorting and improvement of public reading materials this year.

Ministry of Education Revises Primary School Regulations (1)

Article 10 Primary schools shall be governed by educational administrative organs at various levels, and their scope is as follows: (1) Provincial primary schools, provincial experimental primary schools, and affiliated primary schools of provincial normal schools shall be governed by the Provincial Department of Education. (2) Municipal primary schools, municipal experimental primary schools, affiliated primary schools of municipal normal schools, and private primary schools in the city shall be governed by the municipal educational administrative organ. (3) Primary schools established in counties, districts, townships, and towns and private primary schools within the county shall be governed by the county educational administrative organ. Primary schools specially established by organs other than the educational administrative organ shall be supervised and guided by the competent educational administrative organ in the locality.

Article 11 Primary schools shall report the general situation of the school's organization, class organization, roster of teachers and staff, and roster of children to the competent educational administrative organ for approval and record within one month after the start of each semester.

Article 12 Provincial primary schools and affiliated primary schools and experimental primary schools of national colleges and universities shall report the roster of children for this semester and the roster of graduated children for the previous semester to the local county and city educational administrative organs for record within one month after the start of each semester.

Article 13 Experimental primary schools shall submit the experimental plan and results to the competent educational administrative organ and forward them to the Ministry of Education on an annual basis.

Article 14 People or organizations organized by people who are not citizens of the Republic of China shall not establish primary schools for educating Chinese children within the territory of the Republic of China.

Article 15 The establishment of private primary schools shall comply with the regulations of the Primary School Law and these Regulations, and shall also comply with the revised Regulations on Private Schools.

Chapter 1 Funding

Article 16 The ratio of school building and equipment for the initial operating expenses of primary schools shall be six to four or seven to three.

Article 17 The distribution of regular expenses of primary schools shall be based on the following percentages in principle: 70% for teachers' salaries, 15% for equipment expenses for books, instruments, sports equipment, teaching aids, and sanitation expenses, 9% for consumable expenses for experiments, stationery, water, electricity, and firewood, 3% for special expenses such as travel insurance, and 3% for reserve funds. The aforementioned reserve funds shall not be used without the approval of the competent educational administrative organ.

Article 18 The standard of primary school funding shall be formulated by the educational administrative organs of each province and city and submitted to the Ministry of Education for record and implementation.

Article 19 The expenditure of primary school funds shall be economical and truthful. The methods of public auditing and other methods shall be formulated by the educational administrative organs of each province and city and reported to the Ministry of Education for approval and implementation.

Chapter 4 Organization

Article 20 Primary school classes shall be organized separately according to the age, intelligence, etc. of the children at the time of admission.

Article 21 The organization of primary school classes shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 7 of the Primary School Law. The number of students in each class shall be 40 in principle, and at least 25.

Article 22 The two-part organization of junior primary schools may be divided into half-day or time-based systems depending on the school's situation.

Chapter 5 Curriculum

Article 23 The list of primary school teaching subjects and weekly teaching time is as follows: (Explanation) 1. Civic training is different from other subjects, and it focuses on daily training. The time listed in the table is the group training time, which is 10 minutes per day (incorporated into morning meetings and other gatherings).

2. Common sense subjects in lower and middle grades include knowledge parts of society, nature, and hygiene (hygiene habit parts are included in civic training).

3. From the fourth grade onwards, arithmetic subjects add abacus calculation.

4. Social studies in higher grades are divided into three subjects: civics (civic knowledge), history, and geography. Time allocation: civics 30 minutes, history 90 minutes, geography 60 minutes.

5. Natural sciences in higher grades include the knowledge part of hygiene (habit parts are included in civic training).

6. Work subjects in lower grades include art, crafts, and operations. Singing subjects include physical education, music, and homework.

7. Schools may reduce the total time by 30 or 60 minutes per week depending on local conditions. 8. Time allocation is based on 30 minutes per section in principle, and may be extended to 45 minutes or 60 minutes depending on the nature of the subject.

Article 24 Primary school courses shall be in accordance with the curriculum standards prescribed by the Ministry of Education, and their teaching shall be implemented in accordance with the general principles of the curriculum standards, teaching general rules, and teaching points of each subject.

Article 25 Local local teaching materials shall be edited by the school or the local competent educational administrative organ and submitted to the higher-level educational administrative organ for approval.

Article 26 All kinds of reading materials for primary school children should be in vernacular Chinese, and primary school teachers should use Mandarin Chinese as the language of instruction.

Article 27 The outline of primary school teaching materials, the national general part shall be formulated by the Ministry of Education in accordance with the provisions of the curriculum standards, and the local special part shall be formulated by the competent educational administrative organs of each province and city and submitted to the Ministry of Education for record and implementation.

Article 28 For the convenience of teaching, experimental primary schools may organize the teaching materials of each subject into joint individual units for integrated teaching regardless of subject, but they must compile another outline and submit it to the competent educational administrative organ for record.

Chapter 6 Moral Education

Article 29 Primary school moral education should be centered on civic training, and teachers should use various activities inside and outside the classroom to actively guide children, and contact families and local public institutions.

Article 30 Primary schools should carry out various group activities to train children's group life, and may guide children to organize simple and easy-to-use autonomous organizations.

Article 31 Primary schools may implement a counselor system for the convenience of individual moral education. All primary school teachers are directly responsible for moral education of children.

Article 31 Primary schools should contact children's parents at any time to discuss practical issues related to moral education and other issues in order to improve the efficiency of teaching and training.

Article 33 Corporal punishment shall not be inflicted on primary school children.

Article 34 The standards and implementation methods of primary school civic training shall be in accordance with the regulations of the Ministry of Education.

Chapter 7 Equipment

Article 35 The location of the primary school should be selected in a place convenient for children to attend school and must have a good environment.

Article 36 The construction of primary school buildings should be simple and solid, suitable for teaching management and hygiene, and should use domestic materials.

Article 37 Primary schools should have sports fields, workshops, or farms and campuses, and their area must be sufficient for application.

Article 38 The desks and chairs used by primary school children should be suitable for the proportion of children's height.

Article 39 Primary schools should strive to enrich the equipment related to hygiene and sports with reference to the school hygiene facility plan.

Article 40 Primary schools should strive to enrich the equipment related to books, instruments, and teaching aids.

Article 41 Primary schools should have various important registers, charts, etc. related to teaching, moral education, etc.

Article 42 The equipment standards of primary schools shall be determined separately by the Ministry of Education.

Chapter 8 Achievement Examination

Article 43 In addition to the usual examination, primary school children's academic achievements are examined through temporary examinations, semester examinations, and graduation examinations.

Article 44 Temporary examinations shall be held by teachers at the end of each month, and shall be held at least three times in each semester.

Article 45 Semester examinations shall be held by teachers at the end of the semester, but the semester examination shall be exempted for the semester before graduation, and the usual achievements shall be used as semester achievements.

Article 46 Graduation examinations shall be held by the primary school principal in conjunction with the teachers of each subject at the end of the study period.

Article 47 The calculation methods of primary school children's academic achievements, physical education examination methods, and methods for children's promotion and retention shall be formulated by the provincial and municipal educational administrative organs and submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval and record.

Article 48 The moral conduct achievements of primary school children shall be based on the achievements of civic training.

Chapter 9 Admission and Graduation

Article 49 The admission age of primary school children is six full years old, but in special circumstances, it may be extended to nine full years old.

Article 50 If there are vacancies in each grade of the primary school, transfer students shall be accepted at any time within two months after the start of each semester.

Article 51 Primary school children may apply for a leave of absence for one semester or one academic year due to special circumstances of physical or family reasons, and return to school after the expiration of the leave.

Article 52 Primary school children may be allowed to transfer or withdraw from school after the school investigates and confirms the special circumstances of physical or family reasons.

Article 53 Primary school children who have completed their studies and passed the examination shall be given a graduation certificate by the school in accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Primary School Law.

Chapter 10 Tuition and Other Fees

Article 54 Primary schools do not charge tuition fees, but may, in accordance with the provisions of Article 16 of the Primary School Law, request the competent educational administrative organ to approve the collection of tuition fees at its discretion according to local conditions. Primary schools that collect tuition fees as mentioned above shall set up more than 40% of the free tuition quotas for poor children.

Article 55 Primary schools shall not use the collection of fees as a basis for compiling the grade level.

Article 56 The necessary school supplies, etc. for primary schools may be issued by the school, or the school or the local educational administrative organ may organize a consumer cooperative to sell them to children at extremely low prices.

Article 57 Primary schools shall not collect any fees from children, except for special circumstances that have been specially approved by the competent educational administrative organ to raise temporary donations for books and buildings from the families of more well-off children.

The Newly Revised Standard Junior High School Textbooks Published by Datong Bookstore

In February of the 25th year of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Education revised and promulgated the teaching subjects of junior high schools, and the table of weekly teaching hours for each subject in each semester. In the same year, the revised curriculum standards for junior high school, civics, physical education, arithmetic, physiology and hygiene, botany, zoology, chemistry, physics, history, geography, and labor eleven subjects were promulgated separately, and it was stipulated that they would be implemented from the first semester of the 25th year, and ordered the education departments and bureaus of each province and city to comply. In February of the same year, a symposium was convened with bookstore colleagues to discuss the points that should be improved in the editing of textbooks and the implementation methods. In order to adapt to the implementation of the revised curriculum standards in junior high schools across the country in the autumn of this year and adopt appropriate textbooks, Shanghai Datong Bookstore specially complied with the various methods promulgated by the Ministry. In addition to deleting all inapplicable textbooks, it also re-edited all new textbooks in accordance with the above-mentioned revised curriculum standards and their improved points to meet the needs of junior high schools at all levels, and crowned them with the words "New Revised Standard" to facilitate identification. In order to comply with the various points for improving textbooks promulgated by the Ministry, each textbook was edited by education experts and junior high school teachers who implemented the teaching of each subject, in order to fully comply with the principles and standards set by the Ministry. Currently, the "New Revised Standard" junior high school textbooks such as civics, physiology and hygiene, botany, chemistry, physics, Chinese history, foreign history, and Chinese geography have been published. Moreover, in order to comply with the Ministry of Education's regulations on reducing the selling price of textbooks, the prices are extremely low, such as civics, which is only priced at one corner per volume. For other books, the price does not exceed more than five corners.

Sports News

Li Huitang Declines Invitation to Join French Professional Soccer Team

Geneva, 25th (Central News Agency) According to news from Paris, after our World Games soccer team drew 2-2 with the strongest professional soccer team in Paris, Red Star, the French team intended to invite our team captain, Li Huitang, to stay in France and join their team as a professional player, with a monthly salary of 2,500 francs and a lump sum payment of 25,000 francs upon signing the contract. However, Mr. Li, as he is about to retire from soccer, has politely declined.

Starting Points for Women's Hurdles and 100 Meters at the World Games

A Record of Our Country's Soccer Team's European Tour

— Written and sent by Li Huitang

(July 5) Although our match yesterday was not particularly brilliant, today's newspapers and public opinion have been extremely laudatory, considering it a top-notch team. At noon, we were hosted at a banquet by the All-India Football Association. Those present were all well-known figures in the sports world, numbering three or four hundred. After the president gave a speech and presented our team with eleven gold commemorative medals, Director Rong and I offered our thanks in succession. After taking a group photo, we dispersed. In the evening, we were invited by an Indian cinema to watch an Indian national film, which included newsreel footage of our match yesterday. It was quite amusing to see a scene of us chasing and running replayed on the screen. During the intermission, I was invited to the stage to introduce each player to the audience. A wave of cheers and applause erupted, and our team responded by shouting "Long live India!" three times.

Victory over the Anglo-Indian Combined Team

(July 6) The second match in Karachi was against the Anglo-Indian combined team, whose strength was even more complete. It rained in the morning, making the weather feel cool, which pleased us all greatly. This is because our team never performs well when the weather is hot and the field is hard. Moreover, for the past ten days in Rangoon, every match has had a light rain, making the field slightly slippery but not too muddy, which is extremely advantageous for our team's performance. This has become a habit, and the reason why our first match the other day was not up to par was not without cause. Although the weather was not ideal today, it still drizzled during the match, but the audience did not hesitate to attend, and the spectacle was no less than the previous day. At the start of the match, our team lined up as follows. The score was 2-1 in the first half, with a final result of 2-1. The scorers were Huitang,

Bao Jiaping

Tan Jiangbai Li Tiansheng

Chen Zhenhe Liang Rongzhao Zhang Xianyuan

Ye Beihua Sun Jinshun Li Huitang Feng Jingxiang Cao Guicheng

Our team did not leave a good impression in the first match, so we changed our formation today. Because Jiangbai had no success in the front, he was moved to the left back, and Yahui was still weak and had not recovered after his illness, so Rongzhao was placed in the center and Xianyuan on the right. The forwards Beihua and Guicheng were assigned to the flanks. Jingxiang, who had injured his knee in Medan, had been out of action for almost a month. His reappearance today provided a tremendous boost to the front line. The field was quite slippery due to the rain. At the start of the match, Huitang scored a goal from the left wing with a clever short pass through the middle. Afterwards, the opponent's counterattack was very fierce. Fortunately, Jiaping was agile and repeatedly saved dangerous shots, divinely and miraculously, as if aided by Heaven. However, after a long defense, they finally conceded one goal from a corner kick. Soon after, our front line became active again, and Huitang scored another goal with a long shot. The score was 2-1 in the first half. After switching sides, both teams attacked and defended, and the situation was tense. The goalkeepers of both sides repeatedly displayed amazing skills, much to the admiration of the audience. Until the end of the game, there were no further gains or losses. Our team's performance improved on this day, especially the forwards' rapid attacks and beautiful shots. Jiaping's strong defense today was praised by the people here. The other players all performed well and were admired. After the match, each player received a silver shield and a small medal. Huitang gave a speech expressing his gratitude, and then we hurried back to the residence to shower and prepare to take the train to Bombay at 8 PM.

(July 7) Karachi and Bombay are located in the east and west, respectively, more than 1,300 miles apart, and the train takes 38 hours to reach. After the match yesterday, we hurriedly showered, packed our luggage, and arrived at the station at 8:30 PM. We quickly had dinner and said goodbye to the well-wishers before departing at 9 PM. The cars had sleeping berths, and five people occupied one compartment, which was not connected to others. Therefore, we could only meet people at the train stations along the way. The weather in Lanping is usually hot, with the scorching sun oppressive. This day and night train journey is the most tiring. Fortunately, it rained continuously today, and it was cool all day. Last night, we even had to cover ourselves with wool blankets to ward off the cold wind. We bought all three meals, breakfast, lunch, and dinner, in the dining car. There were many stops along the way, so we did not feel lonely or suffer the pain of being separated from others.

Draw with Bombay Players

(July 8) Bombay is known as the "Gateway of India," and those coming from the West must pass through this place. I got up at 7:30 in the morning to wash and pack my luggage. Bombay was right in front of me. Many people came to welcome us at the station, including officials from the Football Association, our country's consul, and leaders from the overseas Chinese community. The station was noisy and chaotic for a while. After taking pictures, we left the station and went to the "Jilian" Hotel for a short rest. Then, we went to a welcoming meeting held by the overseas Chinese community. After the formalities were completed, each representative gave earnest exhortations. After the tea party, we returned to our residence to prepare for the last match of our southern tour against the local players in the afternoon. Having been confined in the train for the past two days, we were playing immediately upon arrival today. Given our excellent record of not having lost a single match, we were especially afraid of slipping up in this last match and ruining our previous achievements. Therefore, everyone was in a state of fear and rested as much as possible, not daring to go out for leisure. We went to the field at 5:30 PM. The field here was small, with only about 10,000 spectators. From this, it can be seen that the passion for soccer here is far inferior to that in Calcutta. After shaking hands with the mayor and the consuls of China and Germany, we deployed our formation to face the challenge. The score was 2-1 in the first half, with a final result of 3-3. The scorers were Huitang (2) and Shun (1).

Bao Jianian

Tan Jiangbai Li Dasheng

Chen Zhenhe Xu Yahui Liang Rongzhao

Ye Beihua Sun Shun Li Huitang Feng Jingxiang Cao Guicheng

The two teams faced off and the whistle blew to start the game. Most of the opposing team were soldiers, and their tactics were very similar to those of the British army in Hong Kong and Shanghai. Their skills were good, and their strength was especially abundant. As soon as we made contact, we knew that a strong enemy was in front of us, and it would not be easy to deal with. Everyone was very careful and cautious. In the first half, Yu and Shun successively scored goals. Jiaping was careless and lost a goal. At halftime, our team was leading 2-1. After switching sides, our defense gradually weakened. Due to mistakes by Tiansheng and Jiangbai, they scored one goal in fifteen minutes, reversing the victory. At that time, the weather changed again, and heavy rain poured down, making it difficult to run and kick. Although the forwards repeatedly shot, they were all saved by the goalkeeper, or hit the crossbar, or went too high, or went too wide, as if they were being protected by the gods. It was a critical moment, and we thought that our undefeated record would surely be lost in this last match today, with no hope of escape. Therefore, the forwards became increasingly anxious to shoot, and the more anxious they were, the more they lost their accuracy, to no avail. Fortunately, Heaven does not forsake people. Seven minutes before the end of the game, an opposing defender was penalized for using his hand to save the ball, and Yu successfully converted the penalty kick. However, we had already broken out in a cold sweat. It was really fortunate that we were able to end the game in a draw.

Our team's performance on this day, in order to achieve complete success, was too serious, so it was not very exciting. The forwards were still decent, but the defense's positioning was confused. All three goals were lost due to defensive omissions, which was a pity. However, being able to recover our undefeated reputation from a near-death experience, in the midst of faint hope, was also a stroke of good luck in misfortune. In the evening, the Football Association hosted a dinner and dance party. The music was melodious, the cups clinked, and after a little drunkenness, the dance was graceful. Everyone enjoyed themselves, and they didn't realize how late it was until the clock struck two.

Since we left the country in early May, it has been less than seventy days. We have had 27 matches with four draws and no defeats, dominating the Asian region. Our record can be considered rare and precious. Moreover, the journey has been tiring, and the social engagements have been busy, especially with other matters. Looking back on the past, everything is still vividly before my eyes, which is truly comforting. When I have time, I will often write in detail about my observations during the southern tour and the differences in soccer in various places, to supplement what I have left out in my previous chronicles. I think it will also be something that soccer fans will be happy to see.

Mayor's Cup Soccer Final to be Held on the 30th of this Month

The city-wide open small soccer competition organized by the Small Soccer Association of this city has been progressing very smoothly since it opened on April 26th. The closing ceremony is scheduled to be held at the Municipal Central Small Soccer Field on the afternoon of the 30th of this month. A total of more than fifty teams participated in this competition. At that time, Lianghua team, which represented Shanghai in the National Games small soccer demonstration last year, will reorganize and show off their skills. Lin Baohua Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday; Practiced at the China Club at 5 PM

Mr. Lin Baohua, our country's famous tennis player, along with Mr. Xu Chengji and Mr. Cai Huiquan, took the Italian postal ship "Victoria" to Europe on March 26th of this year to represent our country at the Davis Cup tennis tournament held in France. His wife, Ms. Liang Peiyu, also went to Europe with him. Mr. and Mrs. Lin left England at the beginning of this month to return to China and arrived in Shanghai at 8:30 yesterday morning. They landed at the Qichang Wharf and returned to their residence at 1A Difeng Road to rest. At about 5 PM, he went to the Singapore Road China Tennis Club to practice with Mr. Zhang Dingzhao for about an hour before returning. According to reports, Mr. Xu and Mr. Cai are still traveling in England, and Mr. Zheng Zhaojia returned to the United States in early August to study. Mr. Xu will also return to China this year, but Mr. Cai's return date is still unknown. As for the Davis Cup, although our country suffered defeat, we have gained a lot of sympathy, especially Mr. Xu's skills, which have won praise from Europeans.

Commercial News

Cotton Yarn: Weak Buying Power; Sharp Drop After Rise in Old Cotton; Final Price at 41.5 Yuan; A Sharp Drop of 11 Yuan Compared to Last Month

Yesterday was the last day for old cotton, and the market remained sluggish, mainly due to a lack of buyers. The final price was 41.5 yuan, a sharp drop of 11 yuan compared to last month's peak. This trend is frightening. As for new cotton, Tongji again made a large number of short sales, but the market remained calm. In fact, many retail investors rushed to cover their positions, and Japanese merchants also came in to support the market. The market tightened in the afternoon.

Tongji Makes Large Short Sales

Before the opening of the bidding for standard cotton, old cotton for August delivery was in its final day, and the market was still weak, falling by 55 cents. The situation for distant new cotton was good, and with clear skies and high air, people became even more bearish, with prices falling by 25 cents. After the second session, it was rumored in the market that the authorities were supporting old cotton for August delivery at 41 yuan, preparing to buy 30,000 dan. As a result, market sentiment stabilized, and the panic and mistakes of the previous day were gone. Prices jumped by 1.05 yuan, with distant months improving by 20 cents. However, in the third session, old cotton continued to rise, while new cotton fell. By the close of trading, distant months improved by 15 cents again. As a result, compared to the closing price of the previous day, distant months fell by 5 to 40 cents, while August alone rose by 1 yuan. Tongji and Yuda reduced their long positions significantly, while Mingde and Runkang bought in aggressively. After the opening in the afternoon, the current month declined again. Although Tongji made large short sales of new cotton, the market was still calm. There was not much change after the settlement. By the close of trading, even more people were shorting, and distant months tended to rise. As a result, compared to the afternoon closing price, each month rose by 5 to 10 cents, while August fell sharply by 2.1 yuan. The sales volume of Tongji was 12,300 dan, Jinchang 5,700 dan, Hexing 2,000 dan, Yuda 15,700 dan, Gengfeng 3,900 dan, Shenfei 2,600 dan, Dachangcheng 3,400 dan, Taichang 3,000 dan, Dachang 2,900 dan, and Jinghua 3,700 dan. The purchases were Runkang 10,500 dan, Yikang 6,700 dan, Lianxingchang 3,700 dan, Changhe 2,900 dan, Changfeng 5,300 dan, Xincheng 5,500 dan, Yi 2,800 dan, Changyu 2,700 dan, Dafeng 7,800 dan, Mingde 7,000 dan, Dafu 3,700 dan, Jifeng 2,000 dan, Daji 2,000 dan, and Da 2,900 dan, Shenchang 2,000 dan. The highest and lowest prices for the day are listed on the left.

Factory Inventory of Spot Yarn is Low; Standard Yarn Market is Stable; This Month's Final Price for Yarn is 7.5 Yuan Lower than July; Markets for Other Months Show a Pattern of Strong Near Months and Weak Distant Months

The yarn market fell in the morning but recovered in the afternoon, showing a slightly stable trend. This is because the spot yarn business can still be supported, and each factory's yarn inventory has decreased, so people's hearts are still at ease. However, in general, short sellers, in view of the low cotton prices, have not reduced the pressure. This month is the last day of business. It is said that a certain company alone bought 4,000 bales and sold them to the Sichuan merchants. As a result, the market sentiment turned up in the afternoon, and the final price was 197.4 yuan, which is 7.5 yuan lower than last month's 204.9 yuan.

Standard Yarn Fell in the Morning but Recovered in the Afternoon

Before the opening of the standard yarn market, the overseas yarn and cotton situation was not good, and the atmosphere was dim. Each month continued to fall. After the second session, this month's yarn was the last day of business. It was rumored that Dasheng Factory had successively delivered 4,000 bales of 20-count red Kuixing yarn and was going to buy back the entire amount. As a result, the market trend turned up, gradually rebounded, and distant months rose. By the close of trading, it was heard that the Osaka Sanpin Yarn Market was sluggish and turned soft again. Juxing and Tongfeng sold a lot, but Dede alone bought a lot. As a result, each month fell by 5, 6, and 7 cents compared to the closing price of the previous day, but this month did not move. After the opening in the afternoon, a certain company was preparing to buy back this month's yarn, causing the market to turn stronger, and distant months rose. At the same time, the demand for spot yarn from customers was still healthy, and market sentiment was slightly firm, but sellers continued to put pressure on the market. As a result, each month rose by 3, 4, 5, and 9 cents to 1 yuan compared to the morning closing price. Tongji sold 3,300 bales, Zhongxing 3,050 bales, Yuda 3,400 bales, Dafeng 1,800 bales, Tongfeng 2,100 bales, Changfeng 5,650 bales, Shengyuan 1,950 bales, Hengyi 1,800 bales, and Hexing 1,600 bales. US Cotton Ultimately Depressed Due to Increased Spread Selling

Yesterday, at the opening of the US cotton market, domestic traders and foreign merchants bought, and the prices for each month rose by 3 to 9 points. However, according to reports, there was rain in Oklahoma and eastern Texas, and local merchants and New Orleans sold back their positions. The December futures were around 11.5 cents. Traders continued to buy, and Liverpool and short sellers also bought. In general, demand was mediocre. Ultimately, the trend was depressed due to increased spread selling. Japanese merchants bought heavily when prices fell. The closing was firm. The spot price fell by 11 points, and the futures price fell by 6 to 9 points. The spot price of English cotton fell by 2 points, and the futures price fell by 4 points. The Indian cotton price initially rose due to short covering and purchases by European exporters, but then fell due to long profit-taking. The price of Pingguoer fell by 0.75 rupees, the price of Yumu was unchanged, and the price of Bai Zaxi rose by 0.25 to 2 rupees. The original telegram record is on the left (telegram dated the 24th).

According to a telegram from Bombay, the opening predictions for the 25th are: the price of Bai Luoqi for July-August delivery is 222 rupees, down 1.5 rupees; the price of Bai Luoqi for April-May delivery is 208.5 rupees, down 1 rupee; the price of Aomula for December-January delivery is 189.5 rupees, down 0.5 rupees.

Finance - The Gold Market is Lifeless - Fluctuations of Only Four Jiao Throughout the Day - Resulting in a Slight Drop of One Jiao

The gold market yesterday was lifeless, with only four jiao of fluctuation throughout the day, similar to the previous day, due to the lack of changes in London spot gold. As a result, there was a slight decline. In the early morning, the overseas silver market showed that the British market rose while the American market was flat. Traders said that after the market closed, licensed dealers would add 0.0625, and the market turned firm due to American purchases. The forward silver price in Montreux rose by 1 to 2 li. The exchange rate slightly contracted. London spot gold remained unchanged. The Central Bank's posted exchange rates revealed that both the British and American rates were flat, and the Customs Gold Unit remained unchanged. The standard gold bar price remained at 223.90 yuan. The market opened flat in the morning. After the opening, it rose slightly due to large traders taking advantage of low prices to make limited purchases. HSBC announced that both the British and American exchange rates were flat, and the white silver balance tax rose by 25. At this time, the market was extremely peaceful. However, as buying interest temporarily waned, those who wanted to sell came to close out positions, resulting in a slight decline. The market was extremely flat at noon, and the later market became even more sluggish, with only two jiao of fluctuation, lacking vitality. Yesterday, swap deals were posted by the bulls at 2 yuan. The day's market conditions are recorded as follows:

The opening in the morning was 228 yuan, the same as the previous closing price. Futaiheng, Wanxingshengyuan and Yongna bar prices rose from 7.9 jiao to 8.2 jiao. HSBC announced that the British and American exchange rates were flat, and the white silver balance tax rose by 25. At this time, the market was extremely stable. Qingfa, Yongzhi, Fengyong, Tongtaichang, Qian, Xiang, Dafeng and Heng slightly sold off, gradually falling to 7.9 jiao. After fluctuating, the noon closing was 1128 yuan.

The after-market opened at 1128 yuan. Qiafengyong, although Nadadecheng and Yuanmaoyong sold, was initially flat and then slightly weaker, falling to 7.8 jiao. Futaiheng still took delivery. The afternoon closing price was 1127.9 jiao.

The closing price, based on the Central Bank's standard gold bar price, remained at 1123.9 jiao, approximately 4 yuan higher than the closing price. The registration price for this month is 1124 yuan, for September 1126 yuan, and for October 1128 yuan. The replenishment water for the morning was 1124 yuan. The spot market situation was stable. Tianjin goods were priced at 13.5 yuan, the buying price for smelted (chì) gold was 11 yuan, and the selling price was 14.5 yuan, but there were no transactions. In the swap market, Dachangxiang (bull side) posted 2 yuan to Huixiang for 63 bars and to Fuan for 28 bars.

There were not many transactions in the market. Overall, Shengyuan Yong, Futaiheng, Futaiyong, Yuanmaoyong, Qiafengyong, Shendayong, etc. slightly bought, while Tongtaichangxiang, Qingfayong, Dadecheng, Tongfenheng, Tongfu, Qianchangxiang, etc. were on the selling side.

The day's market conditions were sluggish, opening in the morning at 228 yuan and closing at 1127.9 jiao in the afternoon. The highest was 1128.2 jiao and the lowest was 1127.8 jiao, with only four jiao of fluctuation. The result was a slight decline of one jiao. There are still 924 bar contracts remaining for this month, with a total of five bullish and four bearish parties. There are 2408 contracts remaining for September, with a total of 15 bullish and 17 bearish parties. The total number of contracts for October is 8008, with a total of 35 bullish and 35 bearish parties. The total number of transactions was 469 in the morning session and 231 in the afternoon session.

Although There Were Many Swap Transactions, There Was Still No Change in Foreign Exchange

The foreign exchange market was still mediocre yesterday. Banks and Chinese merchants engaged in many swap deals. In the early morning, the overseas silver market reported that London's short and long-term rates both rose by 0.0625. Traders said that the market was firm after closing, and the U.S. bought above the posted rate of 0.0625. The New York silver market was unchanged. The forward silver price in Montreux rose by 1.5 to 2 li. London spot gold was unchanged. The British rate against the U.S. contracted by 0.125, the British rate against the French rate was unchanged, the U.S. rate against the British rate contracted by 0.1875, and the U.S. rate against the French rate was unchanged. The Central Bank's posted exchange rates revealed that both the British and American rates were flat, and the Customs Gold Unit remained unchanged. The foreign exchange market opened in the morning with the selling price for the near term. The British rate was 1 shilling 2 pence 275 and 40625 paired, and the U.S. rate was 306125 and 1875 paired. Compared to the previous close, both the British and American rates were flat. After the opening, the banks slightly tightened. HSBC announced that both the British and American exchange rates were flat, and there was still no major change. After that, the silver balance tax was announced to have risen by 25. Banks mutually made deals, and Chinese merchants tightened near and sold far. The overall trend was uncertain. In the later market, banks and Chinese merchants still engaged in many swap transactions, and the overall trend remained unchanged. By the close, the actual price for the near term was 1 shilling 2 pence 375 and 40625, and the U.S. rate was 30 yuan 125 and 1875. Compared to the closing price, both the British and American rates were flat. The far-term rates were also the same. Chinese intermediaries still had no activity, only engaging in more swaps.
